Zhejiang Province Temporarily Postpones Cancellation of Subsidy Tax

The Zhejiang Provincial Government previously instructed the Finance Department to review the resolution of the Third Zhejiang Provincial Representative Conference, requesting the Central Government to order the cancellation of the Zhejiang Provincial Subsidy Tax to alleviate the people's plight. After receiving the order, the Finance Department believed that the land in Zhejiang Province was being reorganized. When the new tax law is implemented in the future, the old land tax system will naturally be abolished. However, in the current transitional era, it is necessary to maintain the status quo. A report was submitted to the provincial government, requesting a temporary postponement of the change. The original report is excerpted as follows: "The collection of subsidy tax under the land tax item in Zhejiang Province was established by the Zhejiang Provincial Provisional Assembly in the Land Tax Collection Law in the first year of the Republic of China. It was stipulated that the tribute rice and military rice collected in the past would be abolished. Later, due to the exhaustion of government funds, this large amount of income could not be compensated for in other ways. The Central Senate decided to change the collection to a subsidy, which was still collected at the original tax rate and discounted. This is how the subsidy tax was collected under the land tax item in Zhejiang Province. According to the original rice quota, the annual actual collection of the subsidy tax is about 500,000 shi, with a provincial tax of three yuan and three jiao, totaling a real income of about 1.3 million silver dollars. This is a large item in the provincial treasury's income, and many provincial and county local surcharges are levied under the subsidy tax item based on the shi quota. The expenditures are all necessary for local construction and are not only impossible to reduce, but also often short of funds. The budget is in place and can be restored. According to the original proposal, the subsidy tax belongs to Zhejiang, while neighboring Jiangsu Province also collects tribute grain outside of the land tax, although the name is different, the nature is the same, and the discount is even higher than that of Zhejiang. It is said that the rent reduction in Zhejiang Province has been implemented, and the tax should be reduced along with the rent, which is to take care of the interests of the owners. The Land Tax Law has been promulgated by the Central Government, and the national land tax is being revised in accordance with it. The land reorganization in Zhejiang Province has long been planned and is in progress. In the future, when the reorganization is completed, the new tax law must be implemented, and the old land tax system will be abolished to eliminate the accumulation of historical biases and establish fair, simple, and good regulations to start anew with the people. The current time is a transitional period, and the status quo must be maintained in order to maintain the overall situation. It is proposed to temporarily postpone the change in order to maintain the overall situation."

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Zhao from Hujiaqiao Kidnapped for the Second Time: Zhao Xichang, who previously opened an oil mill in Hujiaqiao Town, was kidnapped by bandits last year and spent a lot of money to redeem himself, and had no intention of doing business. Unexpectedly, at 7:00 a.m. the day before yesterday (the 25th), his mother, Qin, and his younger sister, Ergou, hired a boat to Songjiang to purchase clothes and other items for a happy event. At around 11:00 a.m., when the boat passed the Majingqiao area near Huan'an, it was suddenly encountered by two bandit boats. The bandits claimed to be searching and forced the boat to stop. More than a dozen burly men, all wearing Zhongshan suits and carrying box guns, boarded the boat, kidnapped Qin and her daughter, and looted their luggage and silver dollars, then sailed south. Their whereabouts are unknown. Upon receiving the report, their family immediately sent people to the police and government agencies to request rescue.

Review of the Irregularities in the Rice Price Stabilization Case: The county government ordered the Rice Price Stabilization Bureau to submit a report for review regarding the alleged irregularities in the rice price stabilization in the ninth district of this county. In order to be cautious, the bureau convened a meeting on the 26th to review the accounts of the rice price stabilization in the district. It was reported that the review revealed that the district sold only 780 bags of rice for more than 4,000 yuan, which seemed too much. According to the report, the number of rice purchases and the invoices from the rice shops did not match. The district office announced on the 25th that the funds were exhausted and the rice was gone, but on the 26th, it reported the purchase of 360 bags of rice, which was even more conspicuous. An item for wine expenses was listed in the accounts, which was inconsistent with the purpose of rice price stabilization. It was decided to report the seven items to the county government and request that they be transferred to the judiciary for thorough investigation. Furthermore, Sun, the director of a certain rice distribution point in the district, privately sold four bags of rice for price stabilization to the Beihuitong Rice Shop in this city. The district itself investigated and reported the facts to the county government for review.

Dianshan Town Robbed by Bandits: Dianshan Town, located at the junction of Punan, Songjiang, and Jinshan, was robbed by sixteen or seventeen bandits, all carrying guns, on the night of the 26th. The Qian family suffered the greatest losses, and the bandits attempted to kidnap their female family members. They were extremely frightened and fled, but the bandits chased after them, causing them to fall into the water and die. The County Public Security Bureau has reported the details by long-distance telephone, and further investigation is awaited.

Suzhou

Appeal Judgment in the Case of Burying a Brother Alive: Guan Maoda, the 13-year-old son of Guan Liukun, a villager in Zeziwan, Minong Township, Baoshan County, was premeditatedly killed by his cousin Hou Genbao on the eighth day of the fourth month of the lunar calendar this year. Hou buried the corpse in the small earth embankment near the Tanziwan tomb mountain to destroy the evidence. After the case was discovered, the Shanghai Jiaotong Road Police Precinct arrested Hou and sent him to the Shanghai Local Court. On June 21, he was sentenced to death. Hou refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court. On the previous (23rd) day, Judge Huang Bingdao of the Third Criminal Tribunal concluded the trial. Yesterday (27th) afternoon, he came to the court to announce the judgment. The original judgment regarding the crime was revoked. Hou Genbao was sentenced to life imprisonment for the crime of premeditated murder, deprived of public rights for life, and iron hammers and wooden hammers were confiscated. After hearing the judgment, Hou Genbao declared in court that he did not accept it and would appeal to the Supreme Court.

Yang Huiru Died from Burns: Yang Huiru, a graduate of the Female Sericulture School in Huguan, 20 years old, from Wuxi, was working at the Dayou Seed Breeding Farm. On the previous (24th) day, when she was measuring silkworm seeds, she accidentally left a fire seed in the fire wine, which burned her whole body and destroyed all her clothes. She was sent to Boxi Hospital in Tiancizhuang and died of serious injuries the night before (26th).

Bandit Intrusion in Wujiang County: Bandits are rampant in the Binhu area of the tenth district of Wujiang County, and residents cannot sleep peacefully at night. Middle-class families have moved away one after another, and those who remain in the countryside can only be slaughtered like fish and meat. The roads are full of thorns, and there is no way to complain, which is regrettable. Tracing the reasons, the collusion and enticement of local ruffians is the biggest problem. It is said that among the six or seven miles of the most famous areas in the vicinity of Lujiabang and Wulu along the lake are Wu Xuqian, Dwarf Da, Fan Asan, a fisherman from Shuangtaqiao, and a wooden figure carver from Xiaoyanggang, all of whom have joined the gang. In addition, Shi Aru and Shi Baolin from Lujiagang, Laoqiezi from Caishen Pavilion, Mao Erbao from Tingzigang, Ni Dabao from Nijiagang, Blind Shen Shusheng from Wulu, and Tang San, a monk from Wujieting, usually gather to gamble, sell cigarettes, and hide bandits. These people communicate with each other, with titles such as "resident scout" and "errand runner." Because these people are all locals, they know who can be kidnapped and who can be robbed, and they have long planned it out. They act as accomplices for the bandits, secretly guiding them. After the event is completed, they divide the spoils and live a carefree life. The local residents value their lives and property, so they can only keep silent. Recently, on the night of the 13th of this month, Sheng Zhusheng from Wujieting and the Chen family who opened a bow shop in Nijiadun were robbed, and it is said that they were all related to these people. What is even more serious is that it is said that the hostages kidnapped in Lüjiawan, Zhejiang, were hidden in Mao Erbao's house in Tingzigang, where they ate, drank, gambled, and spoke without restraint. When the Suzhou Water Police Patrol team arrived at Wulu and heard about the matter, they arrested Mao and sent him to the Damiaogang Public Security Bureau for detention pending transfer to the county. However, a certain principal of a certain elementary school publicly vouched for him, so Mao Erbao was able to escape. Although public outrage was aroused and public opinion was boiling for a time, no one dared to do anything.

Wuxi

Jiangyin Property Bureau Appeals for the People: The Jiangsu Finance Department issued a notice to all counties a month ago, ordering them to continue to levy an additional two yuan per shi when collecting the winter tax this year, according to the method of the 16th year of the Republic of China. The Wuxi County Finance Bureau has already received the order to comply. However, various groups and institutions in Jiangyin believe that the taxes in Jiangsu counties are the heaviest in the country, and coupled with years of disasters and banditry, the people are struggling to survive and cannot bear the burden of additional tax. After a joint meeting, it was decided to jointly appeal to the provincial government and the Finance Department by the Property Bureau and various groups, requesting them to withdraw the order. Yesterday, they also forwarded a letter to the Wuxi County Government and neighboring counties, requesting them to proceed in unison.

A Boat Robbed Mid-Journey in Changshou Town: The boat that travels daily between Wuxi and Changshou Town in Jiangyin was sailing from Changshou to Wuxi at 6:00 p.m. the day before yesterday. At 8:00 p.m., when it arrived near Qianmabridge in Huangtang Township, eight or nine robbers with painted faces and carrying pistols and wooden sticks suddenly appeared and ordered the boat to stop. They boarded the boat and looted it for half an hour before taking the loot ashore and leaving with a shout. After the incident, it was checked that the boat owner, Xu Zengrong, was robbed of more than 30 silver dollars, and the boat crew and others were robbed of more than 4,000 copper coins. The passengers, Wu Amin, was robbed of 24 yuan, Wu Baoyuan of 15 yuan, Chen Genlin of 10 yuan, and Wu Aji of three bolts of factory cloth and fifty bolts of Hengfeng twill cloth. According to statistics, the loss was about 200 yuan. Yesterday, a list was opened and reported to the county for investigation.

Tongrentang Sells Poisonous Smoking Cessation Pills: The county government of this county received a secret report yesterday that Kyoto Tongrentang Pharmacy, near Xiaosifang Alley outside the North Gate, was secretly transporting and selling poisonous pills. County Magistrate Pan, upon receiving the report, sent Judicial Director Zhang Guangrong and police officer Du Cailin to the pharmacy to search it. They found a jar of poisonous pills with about 100 pills near a boy about thirteen or fourteen years old. The pills were larger than red pills and were made of earth skin. The boy and the poisonous pills were sent to the county for questioning. At the same time, Hang Xienan and Zhang Yunxuan, who purchased the poisonous pills, were also sent by the Public Security Bureau. Zhou Chengshen, a member of the staff, opened a court to question Hang and Zhang. Hang and Zhang confessed that the pills could treat stomach gas pain and epidemic diseases, so they went to purchase them and did not know that they were poisonous pills. The boy confessed that his name was Zheng Chenxun and that the poisonous pills were made by his father, and that there were many shareholders, but he did not know the names of the shareholders. After the questioning, Zheng Chenxun was ordered to be detained, and Hang Xienan and Zhang Yunxuan were released on bail.

Three Robberies in a Row, Bandits Arrested: Residents Jia Axing, Jia Rongkui, and Jia Wangshi in Jiawanli, near Dongjiushu in the fourth district (Kaiyuan Township) of Wuxi, were all farmers. At about 1:00 a.m. yesterday (27th), seven or eight bandits suddenly appeared, carrying weapons and speaking in a Jiangyin-mixed accent. First, two bandits used a large stone to break open Jia Axing's gate, and then let the bandits in to loot. The bandits were not satisfied and continued to break into the houses of Jia Wangshi and Jia Rongkui next door to loot. After an hour, they left with the loot and a shout. When the bandits were robbing, Jia Axing's wife, Tu, and Jia Wangshi rushed to the ninth branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge and asked them to send police to pursue the stolen goods. After receiving the report, the branch chief sent a police officer to pursue them. When they arrived at the Huishan Branch Road, they suddenly met two bandits wearing short clothes and carrying packages on their backs. They immediately stepped forward to arrest them and took them to the bureau. Branch Chief Liu opened a court to question them. The bandits confessed that their names were Gu A'er, from Jiangyin, and currently living in the Jinji Silk Factory workshop. When asked, Lu Baolin confessed that he was from Jiangyin, and the stolen goods were wrapped in packages and placed in the mulberry fields on Yusang Lane, and that there were several accomplices hiding somewhere. After receiving the confession, the branch chief is now sending detectives to arrest them and is also sending police to accompany the bandit Lu Baolin to recover the stolen goods. The loss suffered by Jia et al. in this robbery is valued at about 200 yuan.

Jiangyin

Educational Institutions Should Pay Attention to the Thoughts of Young People: The County Party Rectification Committee, in view of the fact that the Communist Party often uses cultural institutions as places for latent propaganda, and that young men and women are often seduced and harmed, believes that this is a serious matter. Therefore, it specially submitted a request to the Provincial Party Rectification Committee to consult the Education Department and order the educational institutions in each county to pay attention to the thoughts and actions of young students to see if there are any improper behaviors. If they are minor, they should be guided at any time to correct their tendencies. If they are major, they should immediately report to the highest party and government organs in the county for investigation and punishment. If there are communist members lurking inside and concealing the report, the responsible person of the institution will be questioned. In this way, the communist members will have no chance to lurk, the young people will be able to study with peace of mind, and the country and society will be able to enjoy long-term peace and stability.

Evidence in the Huashan Murder Case Examined: The case of Wu Rukang, a farmer from Tangjiaqiao in Huashan, Qiaoqi, who was chopped to death by Xia Ali and others with knives in eighteen places in the spring, has been found to be related to Wu Axi and Wu Xirong. After repeated questioning of witnesses, the investigation has not yet been decided, and the fugitives Wang Ali et al. have not yet been arrested. Yesterday (the 25th), Wu Gu, the mother of the deceased, Wu Feng, his wife, and witnesses Wu Rulin, Wu Bingfang, Tang Rupei, and Xu Manting were summoned to testify. They testified that the deceased stated before his death that the fugitives Xia Ali and Wang Bingquan stabbed him with knives, and that Wu Axi and Wu Xirong were accomplices. After the questioning, they were ordered to order the fugitive criminals to return to the case for punishment.

Refugees from Lianshui Fear Bandits and Flee to Xiyangqiao: The day before yesterday, 1,536 refugees from Lianshui arrived, mostly coming by water. It is said that they were not caused by famine, but by the daily killings and arson of bandits, and the people could not bear it, so they sought refuge in neighboring counties. After being escorted to the border of Wuxi by the security forces, they left.

Lin Xiangtai Receives Extortion Letter: Lin Zhaoxiang, the owner of the Lin Xiangtai Oil, Wine, and Sauce Garden at the entrance of Beitaitan Lane, received a letter delivered by the local post the day before yesterday, claiming to be from the reorganized faction commander, asking to borrow 500 yuan. The letter stated that the money should be placed in the yellow stone pile under the Junshan short wall. Lin immediately replied that he was afraid that the money would be taken away by cricket catchers if it was placed in the yellow stone pile, and that it would be best to negotiate in person. He then received another letter stating that he could rest assured that someone was watching the mountain. At 3:00 p.m. on the 25th, the second detachment of the Chamber of Commerce heard about it and sent members such as Lu Wanyun to guard the area in plain clothes. They caught Lu Jianchao and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for handling.

The Bandit Concubine is Captured Again: In the summer of this year, the Zhouzhuang Security Corps searched Xiaorifeng and captured Lu Zhanglin, a bandit, and his concubine Li Zhangdi and her father Li Ruren. Changzhou

County Magistrate Wu to be Acting Director of the Suzhou Civil Affairs Department: Hu Pu'an believed that County Magistrate Wu Deyao of Wujin County had been competent since he took office, so he proposed at the provincial government meeting on the 26th that he be changed to acting director. The resolution was passed.

Six-County Joint Defense Office Approved: Recently, County Magistrate Wu of Wujin believed that the banditry was rampant and that it was necessary to contact each other. He convened Danyang, Yixing, Yangzhong, Jiangyin, and Liyang counties to organize a large-scale six-county military-police joint defense office. Commander Wu of the army was publicly elected as the director of the office, and the county magistrates of each county were the branch directors. A telegram was also sent to Commander Xiong, the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in the three provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, and Director Hu of the Civil Affairs Department to request filing for record. It is now known that Commander Xiong instructed County Magistrate Wu yesterday to approve the filing for record.

Zhenjiang

Two Elderly People Tragically Burned to Death

Inside Caojia Alley, Yantou Street, in the city, a fire suddenly broke out at 3 AM last night, destroying more than ten thatched-roof houses. An old man, Sun Deqing, 81 years old, was burned to death, with only his head and abdomen remaining. His elderly wife was also severely injured. A 69-year-old childless old woman, Madam Wang Huang, was also burned to death. The above two corpses have been examined by the relevant Public Security Bureau after a request from the court, and they have been collected and buried separately.

剿匪指揮部 Executes Seven Bandits

Li Mingyang, Director of the Provincial Security Department and concurrently Bandit Suppression Commander of Jiangsu, ordered the Military Law Department to execute the bandit He Guofan, who looted firearms from the Zhenjiang Lunshan defense corps, as well as six Taihu bandits: Wang Heshang, Wang Xiaochen, Zheng Youen, Liu Xueshi, Li Changyin, and Yu Changqing, who had previously kidnapped for ransom and robbed the Dongshan Steamboat, and looted police and military equipment. They were taken from the county prison at 8 AM yesterday morning, their identities were verified, and they were escorted to the execution grounds at the North Gate to be shot.

High Asset Bandits Rampant Again

In the Xizhaizhuangshan area of Gaizi South Township, the bandits have become rampant again in recent days. Every night, groups of thirty or forty or seventy or eighty bandits commit arson and robbery, stopping at nothing. The people of the township, at this time of the autumn harvest, are suddenly suffering from banditry and are in a state of panic. They are all asking the local militia for protection, and each village has selected more than twenty strong young men to supplement the militia for defense.

Provincial Capital to Have Large-Scale Entertainment

Previously, all gatherings and entertainment performances in the provincial capital were undertaken by local schools and institutions. There has never been a large-scale event. This time, the Provincial Capital All Circles Comforting the Frontline Soldiers Association and the War Zone Disaster Relief Executive Committee, in order to increase fundraising and promote art, specially organized an entertainment committee under the association. Zhenjiang Middle School, Women's Vocational School, Provincial Women's Association, National Martial Arts Hall, Agricultural and Mining Hall, and other institutions are responsible for committee work, and the Agricultural Hall is promoted as director to carry out all activities. It is heard that in addition to inviting famous schools, groups, and individuals in Zhenjiang to participate in the performance, Zhang Pengzhou will also be sent to Beijing and Shanghai to contact entertainment groups to perform in Zhenjiang. The association has scheduled performances to be held at the Zhenjiang Grand Theater on the 27th, 28th, and 29th of this month.

The former Langshan General Military Headquarters in Tongyi was previously occupied by Ma Haishan. The Ministry of Military Affairs ordered the county government to recover it. County Magistrate Zhang, because Ma held a certificate from the official property office, submitted it to the ministry for verification. Dasheng Yarn Factory Distribution of Dividends Issue

The Dasheng Yarn Factory in Tangzha had a surplus of over 800,000 taels last year. A problem arose in the distribution of dividends to employees. After negotiations with Cai Tingnan, the manager of the factory, he agreed to distribute dividends equivalent to seventeen months' salary, which is expected to be resolved.

The Provincial Government sent Yu Can, the fourth section chief, to Tongzhou to collect the monthly rent from Zhang Jian's confiscated property, totaling 25,059 yuan by the end of August. Because the Asset Management Office borrowed 17,000 yuan, it must wait until the busy season surtax is collected before it can be allocated. The remaining amount will be transferred to the provincial government.

Lu Haifan, the chief of the Hekou Public Security Branch in Rugao, was accused of neglecting his duties. Liu Changyan Did Not Complete the Handover and Fled

The county government of this county reported to the Finance Department the handover situation during the tenure of Liu, the former county magistrate, because Changyan, the former county magistrate Liu, did not complete the handover. I learned that the county government had previously received instructions from the Finance Department that Liu Changyan should still pay the difference of 4,275.81 yuan in income and expenditure, and the Finance Department would send instructions to Liu Changyan, the former county magistrate, ordering him to come to Rugao to reconcile the accounts and complete the procedures as soon as possible. Unexpectedly, Liu Changyan was nowhere to be found and fled. The instructions could not be delivered, and a report has been submitted to the department for review.

Huzhou

All Prisoners Must Keep Their Hair on Top of Their Heads

The Wuxing Local Court and County Prison in this city received an order yesterday from the Provincial Local Court stating that, in light of the recent cases of prison escapes, it is due to the negligence of the responsible officers and the lack of special identification of the prisoners. According to regulations, prisoners serving sentences of imprisonment or detention have traditionally kept their hair on top of their heads in a circular, inch-long style in order to identify them and prevent abuses. Recently, new and old prisons have not uniformly kept the aforementioned hair style for identification purposes. In addition to distributing this order, the court urgently orders the prison director and others to comply with it. From the date of receipt of this document, prisoners must uniformly keep their hair on top of their heads for identification purposes, and they may only be allowed to shave it off on the day of their release after serving their sentence. The court must earnestly comply with this order and report back.

Pinghu

Bandits Rob Again in Shantang Town

Shantang Town (under Jiangsu jurisdiction), located about six li from Xincang, was suddenly attacked by sixteen or seventeen bandits led by Zhu Luo, A'mei, and Shen A'jin, subordinates of Taibao Shu, late in the evening of the 23rd. They went to the town with guns and stormed into the home of Huang Sihe in the north of the town to rob. At midnight, six more bandit ships arrived with a total of about sixty or seventy people. After the robbery, they headed towards Mingzhu Nunnery. At that time, there happened to be four Jiangsu provincial water police patrol boats stationed there. They encountered the bandit ships and immediately attacked, engaging in a battle for about an hour. One helmsman was killed and two others were injured on the water police boats. In the end, they were outnumbered and retreated. The bandits then entered the port and headed east via Shantang. Later, the water police gathered a large force at Qiuyi Temple to track them down, but it was too late.

Jiaxing

The Dispute Over Feng Erguan's Drowning Death

A male corpse was found floating in the Zhongshi River in Wangdian Town, Jiaxing, at around 6 PM the day before yesterday. Later, Feng Zhitin and others from Xishi recognized the corpse as that of his clan brother, Feng Erguan, who had gone missing on the afternoon of the 22nd after selling three sheep at Zhang Yongyuan's sheep market on the Nantang shore for 20 yuan. Zhitin reported this to his mother, Madam Feng Zhang, who came to the scene and confirmed the identification. A report was sent to the local court through the town's Public Security Bureau. On the 25th, Prosecutor Liu, accompanied by coroner Guan, went to the town to conduct an examination. The examination confirmed that he had drowned before death. The clan members of the deceased suspect that Feng Erguan had a feud with a certain person, and that he was seen walking with that person on the day he disappeared, leading to Feng Erguan's disappearance. It was not until the 24th that his corpse was found in the river. Therefore, there is suspicion as to whether he was pushed into the river or accidentally fell into the river. It is learned that Madam Feng Zhang filed a petition on the 27th, requesting the court to summon witnesses and arrest the murderers in order to clarify the situation.

The Former Public Security Bureau Chief is Accused

Recently, it was reported that Mo Runxun, the former chief of the Jiaxing Public Security Bureau, was accused of illegally conscripting laborers by the local community and was sued in court. The case has now been transferred to the Hangzhou County Court for trial and has been heard multiple times. Yesterday, the Hangzhou Court summoned the plaintiff, Xu Ajin, the defendants, Fang Zhuangyou, Mo Runxun, and Qiu Zeshen, and the witnesses, Lu Chujue, Huang Tongsheng, Jiang Fuqing, Zhang Ximin, Pu Shuce, and Wu Jinyuan, for questioning. However, the defendant Mo Runxun did not appear. After the interrogating official questioned each witness in detail, he also questioned Fang Zhuangyou and Qiu Zeshen briefly. The interrogating official, due to Mo Runxun's failure to appear in court to defend himself, adjourned the court and ordered Mo Runxun to be summoned for further questioning next time.

Jiashan

Prison Escape Convicts Selectively Executed

The warden of the county prison discovered the day before yesterday that there were eighteen prisoners in the main prison who had filed through their shackles. After a detailed investigation, Lu, Shen, Zhao, and three other prisoners who were found to be the ringleaders in the planned escape were sentenced to death and executed by firing squad at 8 AM on the 26th outside the North Gate.

Tianren Kidnapping Victims Escape Danger

Tianren Town was looted by a group of bandits led by Taibao Ashu on the 7th of this month, and six people were kidnapped: Pan Zhaopeng, the son of the owner of Jiashan Hengtaifeng Cloth Shop; Cen Yongmao and Qin Jiren, employees of the town's Hengchang Money Shop; Zhou Zipei, the owner of Qinghao Tizhuang Store; Gu Zhongyu and Xu Yongli, employees; and Xu Mao, the owner of a foreign goods store. Gu Zhongyu had already escaped earlier. It is now learned that Pan Zhaopeng, Zhou Zipei, and Xu Mao escaped on the 24th after being intercepted by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters stationed in He and have returned.

Shaoxing

The Court Investigates the Village Chief for Embezzling Public Funds Case

Kong Baiyi and more than fifty other village chiefs and neighbors of Tianshui Village in Shaoxing jointly sued the village chief, Li Songnian, to administrative and judicial organs for embezzling thousands of yuan in public bonds and land reporting fees. After the court investigated the case yesterday, it was found that the village collected 475 yuan in public bonds but only submitted 50 yuan to the county. Li Songnian confessed that the rest was with him for the purpose of running a school. In addition to ordering further investigation of other items, the court determined that the village chief's crime was conclusive and ordered him to provide 400 yuan as bail, with Qian and Liang as guarantors, in order to recover the embezzled money and impose punishment.

The Shangzao Robbery and Assault Case is Cracked

After the Shangzao Wharf robbery and assault case occurred in Shaoxing on the night of the 20th, the investigation team went to investigate. The victim was Jinchang Rice Shop. When the robbers came, the shop had not yet closed its doors for the night. The bandits immediately grabbed the shop owner, Wang Yougen, and forced him to hand over silver dollars. The bandits guarding the door fired shots to intimidate. Wang Yougen, in order to save his life, handed over all 142 silver dollars, 297 small silver coins, and a check from Chuhe Money Shop, and was robbed. A stray bullet injured Pan Deyi's right arm, who lived opposite the shop. After the robbery, the bandits sneaked into the city on the 21st and hid in the Jinsheng Hall Inn on Baozhu Bridge. Team leader Li Bichang sent detectives in disguise to arrest them. Unexpectedly, all the bandits had gone out. Zhou Xiaowen, a native of Sheng, was captured on Jiwu Bridge. Under interrogation, he confessed that he had committed the robbery with a certain three people, and that the handgun had been handed over to Squad Leader Zhou of the patrol team. The investigation team immediately transferred the bandit to the Public Security Bureau. After questioning by the bureau, the squad leader Zhou confessed that he had hidden the gun in his concubine's residence behind Fushan Mountain. Police were dispatched overnight to search and found two wooden-cased guns and more than forty bullets. Zhou Xiaowen also confessed that Zhou, the squad leader, was given one of the five shares of the loot. Zhou Zhangshui said that he only received five yuan. Director Mo has now dismissed Zhou Zhangshui and sent him and Zhou Xiaowen to the Provincial Security Department for strict punishment. In the meantime, the search for the remaining bandits is ongoing.

Building the Shelter from Wind and Rain

In the case of building the Qiunü Shelter from Wind and Rain on Fushan Mountain in Shaoxing Prefecture, the initial budget was 1,100 yuan. It is now proposed to completely convert it to cement, exceeding the budget by more than 780 yuan. The Construction Bureau discussed the matter yesterday and decided to temporarily borrow from the construction fund to proceed with the construction and have the county government raise funds to repay the loan.

Local News

Ministry of Finance Requests Subscription to Customs Treasury Bonds

Separate Letters Sent to Various Groups and Industry Leaders

The Ministry of Finance has issued 50 million yuan of short-term customs treasury bonds for the 19th year of the Republic of China, which has been approved by the National Government. Fund raising has begun in August of this year. The principal and interest of the fund are guaranteed by increased customs revenue. Yesterday, Minister Song, Deputy Ministers Zhang and Li of the Ministry of Finance, and the Bond Fundraising Committee of the Ministry of Finance sent separate letters to various commercial groups and industry leaders in the city, requesting them to actively subscribe. The two letters are transcribed below:

Minister Song's Letter: Respectfully, I am writing to inform you that the Ministry has issued 50 million yuan of short-term customs treasury bonds for the 19th year of the Republic of China in order to adjust financial finance. The National Government has promulgated the regulations for this matter. These treasury bonds have an monthly interest rate of eight per cent, and the principal will be repaid starting in August of this year. The principal and interest to be repaid are specifically designated to be allocated from the increased customs revenue. The Director-General of Customs is specifically ordered to allocate funds monthly according to the principal and interest repayment schedule and deposit them in the Central Bank for the Jianghai Customs Two-Five Surtax Treasury Bond Fund Management Committee to act as custodian for payment. The fund is extremely stable, the interest rate is very favorable, and the principal is repaid monthly within a very short period, making it very convenient for the bondholder. In the past, the Ministry has issued various bonds, and we have always been grateful for your willingness to subscribe and your patriotic fervor, which we have long admired. The government has always fulfilled its obligations to repay the principal and interest on bonds issued to the public on schedule. For example, the Jianghai Customs Two-Five Surtax Treasury Bonds were fully repaid in December, and the first batch of cigarette tax treasury bonds will also be fully repaid by November of this year. We strive to ensure the stability of the fund, so the prices of various bonds circulating in the market are rising daily, and the credibility is evident. It is conceivable that the issuance of short-term customs treasury bonds now depends even more on your strong support to help us achieve this great undertaking. Therefore, after careful consideration of the situation, we have divided the subscriptions into different levels and plan to request you to subscribe to a certain amount of these treasury bonds and remit the funds on time to meet our urgent needs. The amount set is particularly reduced compared to previous amounts, and we hope that you will comply. Thank you very much. Sincerely, Song Ziwen, Zhang Shouyong, Li TiaoSheng, Sincerely.

Letter from the Fundraising Committee: Dear Sir, With reference to the Ministry of Finance's letter entrusting your committee to solicit subscriptions for the short-term customs treasury bonds for the 19th year of the Republic of China, we have received your letter of September 11th in response, which states that you have convened a meeting to discuss the methods of implementation, etc., which demonstrates your deep sincerity and support, for which we are deeply grateful. The Ministry has issued various bonds in the past, such as the Jianghai Customs Two-Five Surtax Treasury Bonds, which were fully repaid in February of the 18th year, and the subsequent Two-Five Surtax Treasury Bonds, which were repaid with principal and interest on schedule. The first batch of cigarette tax treasury bonds and interest will be fully repaid by November of this year, and the subsequent cigarette tax treasury bonds have also been repaid by more than half. Other bonds, such as the customs treasury bonds for the 18th year of the Republic of China, the demobilization treasury bonds, and the cigarette treasury bonds for the 19th year, are also being repaid on schedule. All public bonds are also being repaid by lottery on schedule according to the principal and interest repayment schedule. The reason for this is that the principal and interest of the bonds are related to the rights of the bondholders and the financial stability of the society. The government upholds national credibility and cares for the livelihood of the people, ensuring the stability of the fund and never delaying repayment, thereby establishing a good reputation and demonstrating great credibility. This is the Ministry's commitment to maintaining the credibility of the bonds it issues, which should be well known to all Chinese people. The interest rate of this short-term customs treasury bond is favorable and the term is short, and it is guaranteed by increased customs revenue, making it extremely stable. All commercial groups in Shanghai and wealthy patriotic citizens have always been eager to subscribe to each bond issued and have achieved excellent results, for which the Ministry has given separate awards to show encouragement. Therefore, after carefully considering your financial resources, we have divided the subscriptions into different levels and prepared letters to urge you to subscribe. We still ask your committee to strongly guide us so that we can achieve great results and remit the funds to the Ministry as soon as possible to meet our urgent needs. This matter concerns the important policies of the party and the country, and we hope that you will make every effort to do so without any delay. We are deeply grateful.

The Citizens' Association Advocates

Lower Water Rates

Declaration Issued Yesterday

The Citizens' Association issued the following declaration yesterday based on the resolution of the expert committee: The Public Concession Water Company's unprovoked increase of one-fourth of the price has been approved by the Public Works Department, and the Chinese Ratepayers' Association and the Real Estate Association have protested and strongly demanded the cancellation. The water company has only sent a letter requesting the two associations to send representatives to investigate the accounts, but has not expressed any intention to cancel the price increase. This association, as a group of citizens of the special zone, is in a leading position and is dedicated to relieving the suffering of the people. The result of this water rate increase will directly affect the millions of residents of the special zone, and the harm is indescribable. After discussion by the expert committee of this association, the means to deal with the water company are considered unsatisfactory. It was resolved that regardless of the results of the audit, this association will always insist on the original proposal to oppose the price increase. Furthermore, we propose that the price of water must have a fixed standard and must not be calculated based on the amount of rent. The water fee revenue has exceeded several times the increase in rent over the years. From the perspective of social justice, all public utilities must not be for profit, and the price reduction should be implemented to a reasonably low rate to reduce the burden on our citizens, which is fair. Therefore, this case is recorded and announced. The benefit of this matter concerns the personal interests of the citizens of the special zone. We hope that everyone will unite and persist to the end. This association vows to follow this step and strive to be at the forefront for the citizens and to be the support for the two associations, hoping to achieve final victory and seek permanent happiness. This declaration is hereby made.

Letter of Appointment for Reorganization Commissioner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Has Been Issued

Assuming Office May Await Zhang Qun's Return to Shanghai

After the State Council passed the proposal to reorganize the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, appointing Zhang Qun, Li Zhonggong, Chen Xizeng, Wang Yansong, Li Guojie, Guo Le, Huang Hanliang, and seven others as reorganization commissioners, the National Government issued an order. The official letter of appointment was also issued by the National Government's Office of Civil Affairs yesterday. It is reported that Chairman Zhang Qun has resigned, and the National Government is now trying to retain him. Regarding the issue of convening a meeting of the reorganization committee, the commissioners in Shanghai all advocate waiting for Chairman Zhang to return to Shanghai before setting a date for convening the meeting and announcing the assumption of office.

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Actively Proceeds with Reorganization

Board Meeting: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company held its first board meeting at 3 p.m. yesterday. Those present included General Manager Li Zhonggong, Secretary-General Song Shuqiao, Secretaries Chen Zizhen, Zhou Shian, Yu Zhiming, Business Section Chief Shen Zhongyi, Deputy Managers Li Yunliang, He Molin, Shipping Section Chief Huang Penghao, Singapore Manager Cao Renze, Managers of the Four Warehouses Li Gufan, Deputy Manager Li Jingxiang, Industrial Section Chief Fu Jucun, Accounting Section Chief Kong Xiangyu, Deputy Manager Deng Xieren, Administrative Section Chief Lu Qinghai, Treasury Director Wang Yujun, and Recorder Zhang Shoufeng. The meeting was chaired by General Manager Li. First, the chairman delivered an opening speech. Then, the heads of each section verbally reported on the general situation of their respective sections. Subsequently, the meeting discussed the agenda items: (1) Confirming the procedure for implementing the National Government's Regulations on the Reorganization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Contents: (A) From the date of promulgation and implementation of the National Government's Regulations on the Reorganization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the original regulations of the company should be amended in accordance with the regulations. It was resolved to organize a drafting committee for the regulations of the General Management Office to formulate them. Before all regulations are revised, the existing regulations shall still apply, except for those that fundamentally conflict with the reorganization

Page 14

Regulations. (B) The General Management Office shall announce that from the date of implementation of the National Government's Provisional Regulations on the Reorganization of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the regulations, the commissioners of the office have full power to represent the company externally and to execute company affairs. Any external contract or act concluded in the name of the company, or the content of the contract involves the company's assets or other rights, shall not take effect unless signed by the commissioners of the office. However, the office will continue to be responsible for and recognize any contracts legally concluded by the company in the past before the implementation of the regulations. (2) Regarding the cleaning up of share rights and safeguarding investment matters, it was resolved to establish a share rights cleaning up committee. (3) Regarding debt reorganization matters, it was resolved to establish a debt reorganization committee to reorganize debts and consolidate credit. (4) Since there are no fixed regulations for the salaries of crew members, it was resolved that the shipping section should consider the situation and formulate methods to be submitted for approval. (5) Regarding the rectification of coal consumption and materials for each ship, it was resolved that the shipping and administrative sections should jointly formulate rectification methods. (6) Regarding the bulk purchase of coal for stockpiling, it was resolved that it should be handled in advance if funds are sufficient. (7) Regarding how to start construction on the renovation of Warehouse No. 15 and Land No. 64 in the South Warehouse, it was resolved to submit it for review. (8) Regarding the renovation plan and debt repayment methods for the corner building at Fuzhou Road and Sichuan Road, it was resolved to submit it for review. (9) After the Engineering Committee is abolished, should its original responsibilities continue to be maintained by the Engineering Office? It was resolved to temporarily maintain the status quo, except for those parts that have been transferred or must be transferred in fact. (10) Regarding the rental of ships for military service, it was resolved that the business, administrative, and accounting sections should jointly handle it. (11) Regarding internal audit matters within the company, in principle, the audit should be independent. Details shall be formulated by the drafting committee. The meeting adjourned at around 6 p.m.

Military Transportation Transferred to the Administrative Section: Because military transportation requires the requisition of commercial ships, this matter is the responsibility of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in this port. In the past, the task of scheduling and responding to the requisition of ships was the responsibility of Cao Renze, an employee of the business section. Over the past year, Mr. Cao has made considerable contributions. Now that Cao has been promoted to deputy chief of the shipping section, the new general manager, Li Zhonggong, issued an order yesterday stating that the business section has a lot of work, and the two section chiefs, Shen and Li, are already extremely busy handling official business. Now that the ships on the Yangtze River and the sea are officially resuming operations, the responsibilities of the section are even heavier. Therefore, the task of scheduling ships requisitioned by the Ministry of Transportation will be taken over by the administrative section from today to facilitate coordination. The order has been issued for compliance, and the business section is already in the process of handing over.

Resumption of Operations of Sea Vessels: The company's North and South Pacific routes have not been running regular schedules for over a year. This time, with the approval of General Manager Li and the Ministry of Transportation, the sea vessels with passenger cabins will be released back to Shanghai first, with plans to resume regular schedules on the North and South Pacific routes simultaneously. It has been decided that from October 1, the Xin Feng and Xin Ming will be assigned to the North Pacific route, and the Guangli will be assigned to the South Pacific route. The three ships for Fuzhou and Wenzhou will continue to operate, while the routes to Qingdao and Dalian will resume after the Gongping, Yushun, etc., are released to Shanghai.

Dispatching Soldiers for Escort: There are currently six ships sailing on the Yangtze River, and one express ship has also been opened upstream. In order to prevent disturbances by bandits along the way, which hinder travel, the company requested the Capital Garrison Headquarters to increase the number of armed constables on each ship to four to protect them. Negotiations have been ongoing for a long time but have not been implemented. With General Manager Li's telegram request yesterday, the Capital Garrison Commander Gu Zhengtong agreed to allow five fully armed constables to be stationed on each ship to provide protection. The escort will be implemented from today's upstream ships, with a total of 45 soldiers assigned to each ship.

Ship Repair: Among the ships damaged on the Yangtze River and awaiting repair, the Jiangda ship has already been ordered to submit a bid and enter the dock for construction. The Jiangyu ship, which was damaged in Anhui, was towed by the Jianghua ship yesterday and has also arrived in Shanghai and will enter the factory for major repairs immediately. The Emei, which has been repaired, is planned to be sent to the Sichuan River once.

Memorial Service for Mr. Yuan Guanlan Today

The memorial service for Mr. Yuan Guanlan will be held at 2 p.m. today at the Zhonghua Vocational School outside the Upper West Gate. The following is an excerpt from Huang Yanpei's eulogy for Mr. Yuan: "Mr. Yuan's given name was Xishou, and he was from Baoshan, Jiangsu. As a student, he studied at the Longmen Academy in Shanghai, broadly studying classical Chinese culture and also astronomy, geography, and natural history. However, his family became increasingly poor. He often carried books and wore shabby clothes, walking between Songjiang and Shanghai. In the Dingyou year of the Guangxu reign (1897), he passed the imperial examination and became a juren. He served as a professor at the Guang Fangyan Academy, further studying new knowledge and returning to education. In the Gui Mao year (1903), he founded the Baoshan County School. In the Jia Chen year (1904), he and other students from Longmen jointly proposed to transform it into a normal school. In the autumn, he went to Japan to conduct research. The following year, the school was completed, and Mr. Yuan served as its principal. He also planned to establish Fudan Public School and the Taicang County Middle School. He was appointed as the Jiangsu Education Affairs Councilor and the Shanghai General Engineering Bureau Councilor. Subsequently, he accepted the invitation of the Zhili

Yuan Guanlan's Portrait

Education Commissioner to serve as the head of the General Affairs Section and the head of the Library Section of the Education Department. In the first year of the Republic of China, he was summoned by Cai Yuanpei, the Minister of Education, to serve as the director of the General Education Department of the Ministry of Education. He advocated for national higher normal schools and personally went to the provinces to inspect and plan for them. Later, he was reassigned as an inspector. Mr. Zhang Yiqing and Mr. Fan Yuanlian successively served as Ministers of Education and both appointed Mr. Yuan as Vice Minister. For six years, during the declaration of war against Germany, as Vice Minister, he served on the Wartime International Affairs Committee. With Mr. Yuan's efforts, the Shanghai Tongji Medical University was maintained without collapsing. In the seventh year, he resigned and traveled to Europe and America, visiting more than ten countries. He was particularly interested in compulsory education. Upon his return, he promoted it through writing and speaking, and was appointed as the president of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Association and the president of the Jiangsu Compulsory Education Promotion Association. He intended to implement his ideals in one province, but was unable to do so. Therefore, he implemented them in one county and one township. The revision of the national education system and the investigation of the Gengzi indemnity were based on his detailed research and used as

proposals for provincial and county education, as well as important administration. Mr. Yuan treated people with sincerity and was diligent and hardworking in his self-discipline. He was broad-minded and generous in dealing with affairs. His scholarship was unique and rigorous. His demeanor was natural and unrestrained, and his character was lofty. On August 29th, in the 19th year of the Republic of China, he died of illness in Shanghai at the age of sixty-five. In his last two years, he was the director of the Renwenshe (Humanities Society), compiling books. His work was not completed before his death. Therefore, I paint this portrait of Mr. Yuan and write this eulogy: He planned but did not succeed, but he thought for others. His arguments were clear, and his aspirations were high. His contributions to the community were abundant. He called out but was not heard in one country, one province, one village, or one well. However, his teachings were successful. May Mr. Yuan rest in peace."

Increased Cotton Yarn Exports to India

Opportunity to Expand Trade with India

According to a survey yesterday, since the non-violent resistance movement in India, the export and sale of Chinese goods to India has developed considerably. Among them, the progress of cotton yarn is the fastest. Statistics show that over 3,000 bales of cotton yarn exported from this port and sold to India this month. This number has set a new record in history. However, it is expected that the export volume will increase next month. According to the yarn industry, the imported cotton yarn is mainly 42 count, 40 count, and 32 count, and the main import locations are Mumbai and Rangoon, which is a good opportunity for our country's trade with India.

Anti-Opium Association Expands Anti-Opium Publicity

Letter Requesting All National Newspapers

To Publish a Special Issue

The 7th National Anti-Opium Movement Week is scheduled to be held from October 1st to 7th. Preparations have been very busy recently. The association believes that this time coincides with the International Anti-Narcotics Conference to be held in Geneva in a few months. The domestic anti-opium publicity should be more effortful than before. Therefore, it has contacted the news media in major ports across the country in advance to jointly publish a special anti-opium issue during the movement period to facilitate publicity. It is reported that nearly a dozen places in the near provinces, such as the Capital Central Daily News, Zhenjiang Jiangji Daily, Hangzhou Republic Daily, and Wujin Shan Daily, have agreed to publish special issues one after another. Distant provinces such as Tianjin, Hong Kong, Jinan, and Hankou have also sent letters agreeing and have sent the manuscripts in advance. The association believes that this matter should be popularized throughout the country. Yesterday, it sent a special letter to all newspapers, large and small, requesting them to publish special issues during Anti-Opium Week.

Agricultural Inspection Institute Inspects Local Wheat

Implementation to Begin on October 1st

The Shanghai Flour Mill Association requested that measures be taken to ban the long-standing problem of mixing cement and other impurities into wheat. In order to improve the quality of agricultural products and protect public health, the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Institute has reported the situation to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines for approval and will implement inspections in stages to eliminate the long-standing malpractice of fraud. Since the counties north of the Yangtze River are the richest wheat-producing areas, the Gongbei branch office was first ordered to conduct inspections to clear the source of malpractices. Although it has not been long since the Jiangbei branch office inspected wheat in Gaoyou, Guazhou, and Huojiaqiao, the malpractice of wheat fraud has been reduced. The Agricultural Inspection Institute believes that Shanghai is a central location for transportation and sales. The wheat produced in various provinces and counties in the Yangtze River Basin is transported to Shanghai. The malpractice of fraud becomes even more serious during long-distance transportation. If inspections are not implemented uniformly, it will not be enough to prevent long-standing malpractices, which will have a significant impact on wheat quality, agricultural product credibility, public health, and the interests of manufacturers. In view of the above-mentioned circumstances, the Agricultural Inspection Institute has drafted provisional measures for inspecting wheat and submitted them to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines for approval. The inspection and sale of wheat in Shanghai is actively preparing various inspection equipment. It is reported that the institute has ordered various wheat inspection instruments from Japan and the United States, and the preparation procedures are already underway. It has been decided to start inspecting wheat in Shanghai on October 1st. It is also reported that in order to facilitate the inspection of wheat for merchants, in addition to setting up an inspection general office at the institute on Tiantong Road, inspection branch offices will also be set up in Zhabei and the South City. Yesterday, the institute notified the above-mentioned sections to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Flour Mills Association, Miscellaneous Grains Association, and Miscellaneous Grains Exchange and other organizations to instruct their respective wheat firms and dealers to report inspections in accordance with regulations.

Labor Dispute Case of the Steamboat and Wood Industry Union

Arbitration Rescheduled to October 2nd

The labor dispute case in this city where the steamboat and wood industry union demanded that the foremen improve their treatment and revise the conditions was previously submitted to the municipal government for arbitration. The meetings were scheduled repeatedly. At first, the capitalists refused to send representatives, so the arbitration could not be made.

Later, due to a legal interpretation, the municipal government forwarded the request to the central government for interpretation. It has been several months since then. The industry union has repeatedly requested a prompt arbitration so that the workers can work with peace of mind. The arbitration committee scheduled a meeting for the 25th of this month. However, on that day, in addition to the municipal government representative Guo Shen, the municipal party representative Yang Qingyuan, the special district court representative Pang Shurong, and the Shanghai local court representative Wang Qufei, the municipal chamber of commerce representative Zhang Dalian and the civilian training association's labor representative Wu Xiangyun did not attend, and the meeting could not be held. The meeting has been rescheduled for 1 p.m. on October 2nd, and the parties concerned have been notified and the committee members have been informed to attend at that time.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Explains Reasons for Collecting Handling Fees for Cases

To Urge the Organization of Trade Associations

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Yong'an Textile Company yesterday explaining the reason for charging handling fees for entrusted matters from non-members, saying, "In reply to your letter of September 26th, the Chamber of Commerce has registered before and instructed you to join the Chamber of Commerce as a store member. Now, you suddenly treat Chamber of Commerce members as requiring a handling fee of 30 yuan per case for requested matters. You are wondering whether you can continue to join the association. We have investigated that Article 2 of the revised Implementing Rules for the Trade Association Law of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, ordered on July 25th of this year, stipulates that when there are seven or more companies in the same industry in the same region, they must organize an association in accordance with this law. The number of textile companies in this city is more than seven, so they should organize a trade association in accordance with the law and cannot join the association alone as a store member. As for the Chamber of Commerce's previous letter requesting that you be handled as a member of the Chamber of Commerce, this was because the joint organization of industries above one region had not yet been discussed and decided by the Legislative Yuan, so it was still regarded as not having a trade association. Now, the Law on Trade Associations has been discussed and decided by the Legislative Yuan. According to Article 14 of the Amendment, if two or more trade associations

are agreed by more than two-thirds of their members to organize a joint association, then your company is a member of the Chinese Textile Factory Joint Association. However, the organization of a joint association should first organize a trade association in the city where it is located, and then contact other trade associations in various places to organize a joint association to be legal. Now, it has been found that there is no organization of a Chinese Textile Industry Trade Association in this city, and there is only a Chinese Textile Factory Joint Association, which has no legal basis. Based on the above reasons, your company's business is in the same urban area and the number exceeds seven, so you should naturally organize an association and cannot join the Chamber of Commerce as a member. The Chinese Textile Factory Joint Association, which you have joined, cannot join the Chamber of Commerce for the time being because its organization has not been legalized. Therefore, in the absence of remedy, the Chamber of Commerce has adopted a transitional measure of charging a handling fee for a one-year period for each request from industries that have not joined the Chamber of Commerce, in order to promote the organization of various industries in accordance with the law and join the Chamber of Commerce uniformly. We hereby inform you of the above information and hope that you will investigate and handle it accordingly."

Jisheng Society Investigates Liaoxi Flood

The Chinese Jisheng Society has already remitted 10,000 yuan to Suizhong to set up porridge factories and actively provide relief for the flood in Liaoning Province. Yesterday, Mr. Yang Zigong, chairman of the charity associations of the four provinces of Fengtian, Jilin, Rehe, and Heilongjiang, entrusted by General Zhu Ziqiao and Qian Junren, the co-organizers of the relief office, came to Shanghai to report on the disaster. He went to investigate the disaster situation in person and found it to be extremely pitiful. The most severely affected counties and the number of disaster victims he personally investigated are listed below: In Suizhong County, the land is divided into six districts, and more than 30,000 houses were washed away. More than 1,300 people were washed away in the city, and 30,000 houses were collapsed in the four villages. 30,000 mu of farmland were flooded, and there were 70,000 disaster victims. In Jin County, more than 10,000 houses were washed away in Xiguan, and sand flooded and submerged 50,000 disaster victims. In Panshan County, the land is divided into eight districts, and six districts were flooded. More than 20,000 houses were washed away, and there is no hope for the autumn harvest. The water has not receded yet, and there are 120,000 disaster victims. In Xinmin County, the land is divided into eight districts, and six and a half districts were flooded, with 120,000 disaster victims. In Zhaonan County, the entire territory was flooded, with 120,000 disaster victims. In Yi County, two districts were destroyed, with more than 3,000 disaster victims and 200-300 deaths. In Heishan County, there were 3,000 disaster victims. In Chaoyang County, there were more than 10,000 disaster victims. In Zhangwu County, there were 50,000 disaster victims. In Haicheng County, there were more than 4,000 disaster victims. The total number of disaster victims is approximately 6 million. The houses washed away in each county were extremely numerous. Wherever the water reached, the farmland was covered with sand and could not be cultivated. Even the prosperous areas in cities and villages were also covered with sand. The highest place was covered with sand up to one zhang (approximately 3.3 meters), and the lowest place was also 5 chi (approximately 1.67 meters). The urgent relief method requires a huge amount of funds, and the fundamental relief of removing sand from the fields cannot be done without raising huge funds. Now, the disaster victims have no clothes or food, and the situation is even more tragic with the impending cold weather. The magnitude of the disaster and the number of disaster victims are rare in history. We hope that people all over the world will understand this and provide relief and save this catastrophe.

Overview of This Year's Japan Post Business Operations

A Decrease of 6 Million Compared to Last Year

The Japan Mail Steamship Company has already reported the overview of income and expenditure for each route this year from January to September. Due to the sluggishness of shipping operations in various ports, the business in the nine months of this year will be less than 6 million yuan compared to last year, and the expenditure for the nine months will be 33 million yuan according to last year (last year's income for nine months was more than 36 million yuan). Therefore, the company has no surplus profit this year to distribute to the shareholders of each share.

Two Cars Collide, Crossing Arrest Right in the Way

Died Without Timely Treatment

Song Shuqiao's and Sun Baorong's Cars

Collide Suddenly on Avenue Dubail

Two Coachmen Shirk Responsibility

Police Are Drawing Diagrams to Study the Matter

At 8:15 a.m. yesterday, the cars of Song Shuqiao, Secretary-General of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Sun Baorong, Advisor to the Municipal Government, collided at the intersection of Avenue Dubail and Rue Pupier in the French Concession, fatally injuring a crossing guard No. 398 standing there. Song, currently residing at No. 47 Wanjian Lane, Rue Luber, owns a private car No. 1873 (Municipal No. 5230). Sun resides at No. 230 Avenue Dubail and his private car number is 2377. At the time, Song's car was heading north and Sun's car was heading west. The crossing guard was standing on the fixed post made of elliptical cement (with two black and white wooden posts about three feet high on the post) facing east. As Song's car approached from the south, he quickly raised the baton he was holding. At the same time, Sun's car sped from the east directly into the center of the road. Seeing this, Song's driver was unable to brake in time and hurriedly turned the front of the car west in an attempt to avoid the danger of a collision, but it was too late and the car directly struck the crossing guard. The guard suffered severe injuries to his legs and waist and immediately fell to the ground without speaking. The elliptical cement and wooden posts were completely smashed. Other guards noticed and went forward to detain the car and reported to the police station. The crossing guard was first sent to Guangci Hospital, but his injuries were too severe and he died less than an hour after arriving at the hospital. The coachman was temporarily detained at the police station. After questioning by the police chief, Song's coachman stated his name was Yu Jingui, from Ningbo, 31 years old. Sun's coachman stated his name was Sun Zulin, from Ningbo, 33 years old. The two men each described the circumstances of the accident and shirked responsibility to each other. Then, personnel from the car department were dispatched to the scene to draw diagrams for future reference. After the crossing guard's body is examined, a review will be conducted.

Yesterday Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad

Ma Qiyuan Didn't Want the Police to Lose Face

Asked Newspapers Not to Disclose His Number

Before Execution, the Two Criminals Sobbed Together

Ma Qiyuan (aka Ma Jiyuan), a Henan native who previously served as a police officer, was only twenty-eight years old. Around the years of seventeen and eighteen, he colluded with Liu Fuxing (thirty-four years old) from Suzhou and others to repeatedly kidnap people for ransom. Victims included Ye Daming, Xu Fusun, Xu Wusheng, Chen Xiaofu, etc., who were successively kidnapped. Ye was even shot dead by the kidnappers. Ma and others were involved in all these cases. Later, the Jing'an Temple police station arrested them. At the same time, Wang Liangui, Li Afu, Rong Zhengchang, and Shen Shaoqing were also arrested. The former Provisional Court interrogated and sentenced all six criminals to death and reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. The Special District Local Court received a reply from the Provincial Government ordering the execution of Ma and Liu by firing squad. At nine o'clock yesterday morning, Cheng Shangfeng, the execution judge of the Special Court, opened the court and ordered the police to bring Ma and Liu from the West Prison to the court. He announced that the execution was to be carried out today and asked if they had any last words. According to Ma, "I am indeed wronged, but since I have been sentenced to death, I am happy to be executed today. However, as I was a police officer, my execution will inevitably be reported in the newspapers. I request that the reporter not publish my number when I was a police officer in the newspapers so that my colleagues will not lose face because of me." Apart from this, there were no other words. After finishing his statement, he begged for food and drink. Liu Fuxing requested that a letter be sent to Fan Jiantou at No. 251, opposite the Xiaocai Market on Ermalu, asking him to collect the money he had lent out and give it to his mother for her needs. Judge Cheng immediately granted the request. He then ordered an officer to withdraw two yuan from public funds from the accounting department to buy wine and food for Ma and Liu to eat together. After they were drunk and full, the escort detectives escorted the two criminals onto the prisoner car and drove to the Caohejing Jiangsu Second Prison execution ground. The Shanghai Local Court was notified in advance to appoint Prosecutor Wu Shixin as the supervising officer. Then, Police Chief Yang Deshan, Police Inspector Chen Xihui, Supervising Police Wang Jianqing, Xu Guoguang, etc., were ordered to rush to the Caohejing Second Prison execution ground. After the judge took his seat, the two criminals were brought before the court for interrogation. The two criminals sobbed together. The judge immediately ordered the execution. Police Chief Yang commanded the executioner police Gu Hanqing, Yin Daoxu, Xue Bingzhang, etc., to take the criminals down for execution by firing squad. The bodies were collected by the authorities.

Carpenter's Bestial Act

Forcibly Defiling a Thirteen-Year-Old Girl

Then Intimidating Her to Prevent Disclosure

Upon Discovery, When Seeking an Explanation

He Had Already Fled Without a Trace

Wang Zhang, a Nanjing woman, lives in the loft on the second floor of No. 19, Zhonghua Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao, in the French Concession. She is thirty-eight years old. Her husband has passed away, leaving her with only one daughter, named Acai, who is only thirteen years old. She is petite and exquisite, with a beautiful appearance. The mother and daughter are dependent on each other, earning a living by washing clothes for others every day. A neighbor, Mr. Jia, is a carpenter and lives on the third-floor sundeck. The other day (the twenty-first), around six or seven in the evening, Ms. Wang happened to be cooking downstairs and ordered Acai to collect clothes from the sundeck. Jia saw that Acai was charming and moving, and he was immediately overcome with bestial lust. He immediately rushed forward and pressed Acai down on the bed, took off her clothes, and stuffed her mouth, committing an inhuman act. Acai was young and weak and could not resist. She had to let him do as he pleased. Before long, he finished and then threatened her with an axe, forbidding her from mentioning a word of it to her mother. But Acai was not yet fully developed, and after being ravaged in this way, she suffered from alternating chills and fever the next morning, and her lower body was swollen and painful. On the twenty-third and twenty-fourth, she was confined to bed, moaning incessantly. Her mother, Zhang, thought it was just a common cold caused by overwork and paid little attention to it. It was not until dinner on the twenty-fifth that Acai could not bear the pain and told her mother about the rape. Ms. Zhang was stunned when she heard this and rushed upstairs to look for Mr. Jia, but he had not returned for two days. Later, the second landlord paid two yuan to hire a car to send her to Baolong Hospital for treatment. The hospital notified the Dada Mingzhong police station and ordered detectives to investigate. After reporting to the police chief, he ordered the pursuit of the lewd scoundrel for investigation.

Attempted Rape of a Young Girl

Also a Carpenter

Zhang Yunqing, an employee of the inland water company, lives at No. 2, Ren'an Lane, Penglai Road. Because he had just moved in, he hired a carpenter, Qian Youfa, to renovate the house. Yesterday at noon, Mr. and Mrs. Zhang were not at home, leaving their seven-year-old daughter, Zhang Gendi, alone to guard the door. Unexpectedly, Qian Youfa, seeing that there was no one around, was overcome with bestial lust and pinned the child down on a stool, attempting to rape her. Municipal Government Exempts Poor Households from House Tax

Amending Article 13 of the Regulations on the Collection of House Tax

Tenants Are Exempt from Paying Taxes If the Tax Amount Is Less Than One Cent

In order to show consideration for poor households, the Municipal Government has specially added a clause exempting poor households from tax to the House Tax Regulations. The public notice was issued yesterday, stating that Article 13 of the Shanghai Municipal House Tax Collection Regulations has been amended. The text of this order is as follows: Article 13 of the amended Shanghai Municipal House Tax Collection Regulations: This house tax shall be collected by the Finance Bureau, which will send special personnel to collect it from the tenants and issue house tax tickets at any time. Half of the amount payable by the landlord shall be advanced by the tenants and deducted from the rent payable. If a household has moved in for half a season within a quarter, the full tax shall be paid; if it has not reached half a season, half the tax shall be collected; if it is less than fifteen days, no tax shall be paid. For monthly rents of one yuan or less, tenants are exempt from paying the portion of the tax if the tax amount is less than one cent.

Procedures for Reorganizing Charity Group Property

The Property Reorganization Committee of Charity Groups in this city held its second standing meeting yesterday to discuss the procedures for reorganizing charity group property drafted by Mo Heng, a standing committee member of the committee. The procedures were amended and passed. (1) The committee shall prepare a property catalog, including forms for land, houses, savings, and loans, and submit them to the charity groups for registration within a time limit for investigation by the committee. (2) The committee members shall periodically go to the charity groups to check the property books, registers, deeds, and other documents. (3) The committee shall designate a date and notify the charity groups to send personnel to accompany the committee staff to conduct on-site surveys of each place. (4) In the event of disputes over any property, the committee shall solicit the opinions of the charity groups and formulate solutions for each item to be submitted for approval, and then the Social Affairs Bureau shall order the charity groups to comply. (5) If it is deemed necessary to reorganize or change the current method of using various properties, the committee shall solicit the opinions of the charity groups and formulate specific reorganization plans to be submitted for approval, and then the Social Affairs Bureau shall order the charity groups to comply. (6) The committee shall determine the bookkeeping format for charity groups to record property, and the Social Affairs Bureau shall order the charity groups to comply. All investigation forms shall be submitted by the two members, Xu Zhendong and Mo Heng, to the two members, Xu Yongxiang and Zha Renwei, for review and then printed.

Hiding 23,000 Red Pills Inside

Yesterday morning, while walking in a small alley in Lan Nid渡, several hooligans suddenly used the excuse of inviting Wang to tea and dragged him to the home of Wu Youfu, a native of Yangzhou, at No. 29, Changsheng Lane (people generally call it "Stripping Pavilion" because Wu specializes in selling red pills to opium addicts. If poor people who are addicted to opium do not have money to buy it, they can take off their clothes and exchange them for red pills to relieve their cravings). They threatened Wang in every way, claiming that the rice he was carrying was stolen from the ship. They searched him and took away the thirty yuan he had hidden on his person.
