Another Record of Cruel Teacher Abusing Apprentice

The Body Was Not Yet Examined Yesterday

The Children's Welfare Association Sent a Letter Requesting Strict Action

Mo Xianggan, a native of Shaoxing, took Zhao Sangen, a thirteen-year-old apprentice, who was severely abused by Mo, resulting in death due to injuries. Neighbors complained and demanded a thorough investigation. This case was reported yesterday. It is now heard that the Shanghai Local Court has appointed a prosecutor and an examiner to come for examination. After the examination, a coffin should be prepared for burial. However, the body was delayed until 4:00 PM yesterday before being coffined and buried, causing a stir among the people far and near who came to watch in an endless stream. It is said that the corpse's eyes suddenly protruded, and white foam kept flowing from his mouth, which was very miserable. However, his family is far away in Shaoxing, and they had not yet come to Shanghai by yesterday evening. The Chinese Children's Welfare Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Local Court regarding this matter. The original letter is as follows: Respectfully, on September 26, according to a telephone report, Mo Xianggan, a resident of No. 1, Lane 88, Yujia Lane, Xiaonanmen, Nanshi, privately tortured his apprentice Zhao Sangen to death. Please submit a complaint on our behalf, etc. We sent Wang Guanyi, a member of the Security Department, to investigate. It is said that the body of Zhao Sangen, the apprentice who had been tortured to death, was found lying supine, about to be put into a coffin. He was wearing clothes, and no injuries were visible. However, his face was thin and emaciated, and there were two wounds on his head, with bloodstains still present. When asked, the neighbors said that Mo Xianggan was a silversmith by trade and was cruel by nature. He often used iron hammers for hitting silver to strike his apprentices' heads and used very heavy objects to press them down so that they could not move. He also used very thick ropes to tighten their throats so that they could not shout and often forbade them from eating while still making them work as usual. Zhao Sangen's death was definitely caused by being beaten, and his face was emaciated because he was definitely starved. The wounds on his head were definitely struck by an iron hammer. There were also his close neighbors Zhao Gensheng, Zhou Nanrong, Dong Rongxiang, Dong Rongsheng, Wu Fugao, Wu Shangkui, etc., who jointly submitted a report to the First Branch of the First District, requesting a thorough investigation. Jin, the chief of the branch, prepared a document requesting your court to examine the case and issue a burial permit for the injured who died. Based on this investigation, Shanghai is a commercial center, with shops lined up and factories like forests. The number of child laborers and apprentices is very large. Such inhumanity cannot be tolerated. Since your court has accepted the case, you should apply the appropriate articles of the law. For the sake of protecting children, our association dares to seek redress for the deceased and beg for the lives of the living. We earnestly request your court to handle the matter seriously and make it public as a warning. Our association will represent the children of the whole country and kneel and cry out for justice. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Local Court, Chinese Children's Welfare Association.

Sentence Announced in the Case of Selling Daughter into Prostitution

Each Person Sentenced to Separate Penalties

Xu Feng, a native of Changshu, formerly residing at No. 20, Bing'an Lane, Ailai格 Road, French Concession, had previously promised her twenty-year-old biological daughter, Xu Cizhen, to the couple Ling Boyou and Ling Wu as a child bride. But last month, she colluded with Shen Bingsheng and Li Zhongwen to take Xu Cizhen out and sell her to Zhu Zhang at No. 14, Hongyun Lane, Huage聂 Road, as a prostitute, for a price of 300 yuan, which they divided among themselves. The matter was learned by the French Concession police detectives Hang Guangfu and Ding Wensheng, who considered that Feng and others selling a good woman into prostitution violated the criminal law. They arrested all the above people and took them to the police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the French Concession Court for investigation. The Western detective chief first reported the previous situation and questioned Xu Feng, who admitted to selling her daughter without denying it. Ling Boyou and Ling Wu confessed that Feng had sold her daughter into prostitution and that they knew about it beforehand and had shared 50 yuan. Shen Bingsheng and Li Zhongwen confessed that they acted as intermediaries for the people and shared dozens of yuan. Zhu Zhang admitted that she had bought the woman to be a prostitute. The Chinese and Western judges ruled that Xu Feng had violated Article 249 of the criminal law and sentenced her to two years in the women's prison. Zhu Zhang was also sentenced to two years. Shen Bingsheng and Li Zhongwen were each sentenced to four months in the Western prison. The Ling Boyou and Ling Wu couple were each sentenced to three months as a warning. Xu Cizhen was ordered to be sent to the Jiliang Institute for matchmaking and was allowed to sever ties with her parents.

Using Counterfeit Money to Rent a Car

Zhao Bingxian Carried it Out for a Long Time and Was Exposed

Zhao Bingxian, a native of Zhenjiang, liked to hire cars. He often accompanied two or three young men to car rental companies, giving them ten-yuan banknotes from the Bank of China as payment for the car. The car rental company employees saw that he was dressed in a Western suit and behaved luxuriously, and they did not suspect that he was using counterfeit money. Therefore, they did not carefully check the banknotes he gave them. Even after they discovered the counterfeit money later, there was no way to recover it. Recently, the Donghai Car Company on Pingliang Road was fooled by him several times. It was not until the twenty-fifth that they discovered it on the spot and called the police to arrest Zhao. Detective Jin Yangwu of the Yangshupu police station found out that, in addition to the Donghai Car Company, the Huali on Yangshupu Road, the Gongping on Broadway, the Huishan on Shanxi Road, and the Xinhuishan Car Company had all received counterfeit money from Zhao as car fares. Because Zhao's home was located at the intersection of Pingliang Road and the French Concession, Detective Jin went to search his house, but no counterfeit money was found. Yesterday, he was sent to the Special District Local Court, where Judge Feng interrogated him about the origin of the counterfeit money. However, Zhao completely denied using counterfeit money. However, the employees of each car company all stated that the counterfeit money was indeed paid by the defendant. Judge Feng ordered the defendant to be detained pending further investigation and interrogation.

The Bride's Age is Unreliable

The Groom's Family Wants to Cancel the Engagement

Discovered Stolen Steel Bars

Yesterday morning at approximately 2:30 AM, Chen A-long and other detectives from the Songhu Anti-Smuggling Camp discovered a large group of Jiangbei workers carrying a large quantity of steel bars near the Dayang Bridge in the western part of Shanghai. The steel bars were needed for building construction. The workers appeared flustered and secretive. Suspecting that they were carrying the steel late at night for dubious reasons, Chen and his team ordered them to stop for questioning. However, the workers immediately opened fire to resist arrest and abandoned the steel bars as they fled. Chen and his team, outnumbered and facing gunfire (two shots were fired, fortunately missing them), dared not pursue them. They seized the abandoned steel, estimated to weigh over twenty dan. Later, it was discovered that the steel bars were for the construction of buildings inside the Toyota Factory and had been stolen from the nearby Fuxingchang workshop where they were stored. The factory sent representatives to confirm that the items had indeed been stolen. Subsequently, Chen and his team returned all the stolen goods to the factory.

Silk Factories Oppose Public Measurement Inspection

Meeting to be Held Tomorrow to Discuss

Silk factories in the city have been suffering losses due to public measurement since it was introduced. They suffer many losses such as devaluation and being unable to ship on time. They are firmly opposed to it, and the Shanghai Silk Factories Association has sent a letter to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau requesting that the Raw Silk Inspection Office be ordered to stop the public measurement inspection from October 1st, when the trial period ends, in order to protect the silk industry. The Silk Factories Association received a reply from the Commodity Inspection Bureau yesterday, which was immediately communicated to all manufacturers. They all feel that the bureau is disregarding the difficulties of the merchants. Now that the sale of factory silk to Europe has plummeted and the silk industry is facing a crisis of survival, they cannot afford to suffer this unexpected loss. The public is outraged and appeals to the Silk Factories Association to convene a general meeting of all members immediately to discuss further measures to achieve the goal of cancellation. The executive committee of the association has scheduled an emergency meeting of all members for 3 PM on the 29th of this month (tomorrow). A notice has already been issued.

Famous Russian Cyclist Arrives in Shanghai

National Competition with Zheng Longfei at Weile Garden Today

Russian cyclist Semashko arrived in Shanghai recently. Today, he will compete against Zheng Longfei, a famous Chinese cyclist, in a national competition at Weile Garden on Dige Road. The competition will consist of two sessions, one during the day and one at night. Both sides are highly skilled and deserve attention. Details of the competition are as follows: "Russian Champion" Semashko holds the Russian and Harbin championship records. He has won countless prizes, both large and small. His life as a cyclist and his outstanding achievements are admirable. He is here in Shanghai during his travels, and he will show his skills at Weile Garden. Sports enthusiasts should not miss this opportunity. "Zheng's Art" Zheng Longfei is a leading cyclist in China and a pillar of Weile Garden. Although he has only been training for five or six months, and it may be difficult to compete with the veteran Russian champion who has accumulated years of experience, he will at least put up a fierce fight against Semashko. "National Competition" The day session will start at 3 PM, and the night session will start at 9 PM. The competition between Semashko and Zheng can be considered a national competition between China and Russia. The excitement and splendor are extraordinary. In addition, there will be various long and short distance cycling races, motorcycle races, and pacing races. There are more than ten events in total. "Student Discounts" Since the arrival of the famous Russian cyclist, students from various schools have wanted to see him in person. They have written to Weile Garden requesting group discount tickets. However, this is limited to groups. Many students who are interested in practicing cycling are organizing amateur sports classes. The garden will provide free guidance to promote amateur sports and will also give prizes when amateur class competitions are held in the future.

Labor Dispute at Shanghai Silk Factory

Social Affairs Bureau's Mediation Yesterday Yields No Result

The Japanese-owned Shanghai Silk Factory in Caojiadu has been operating for over twenty years and has been very successful. The factory's operations have also gradually expanded. However, on the 17th of this month, a dispute suddenly arose between labor and management, leading to a work slowdown. Party and government agencies have been mediating, but the management's attitude has been extremely tough, making it difficult to reach an agreement. The negotiations eventually broke down. Recently, the management realized that the shutdown was not a good idea and wrote to the Social Affairs Bureau asking them to mediate again. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned both parties for talks and held a mediation session. Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, the second mediation meeting was held. Details are as follows:

Causes of the Dispute: The cause of the dispute between labor and management was the factory's unwarranted reduction of workers' wages, without prior approval from the Party and government. The female workers expressed their dissatisfaction, stating that at a time when the cost of living is rising, other factories are increasing wages. This factory not only does not increase wages, but also wants to reduce them. It has been found that the factory has reduced wages four times in the past few years. The initial wage for each piece of silk was 1 yuan and 10 cents, but it has now been reduced to 36.7 cents. The workers have been silently enduring this, but now the factory wants to reduce it by another 40%, leaving only 22 cents. This has led to widespread opposition, while the factory's attitude remains tough and shows no sign of retreat.

Post-Dispute Mediation: After the labor dispute occurred, Ren Luping, the director of the Sixth District Public Security Bureau, feared that the incident would escalate and repeatedly summoned both parties for mediation, but to no avail. The female workers unanimously expressed their work slowdown starting on the 17th of last month. The Social Affairs Bureau also sent personnel to mediate, but the management showed no sincerity, and the dispute became unresolved. However, the management has now realized the situation and the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is continuing to mediate in order to resolve the matter as soon as possible.

Labor's Demands: The labor unrest was purely caused by management's unwarranted wage reduction. Therefore, labor feels that management should bear the responsibility, and the conditions put forward are: (1) Restore the original wage per piece of silk; (2) Wages should be paid as usual during the strike; (3) Workers should not be dismissed without reason; (4) Workers should be allowed to wash before leaving work; (5) Wages should not be arbitrarily fined; (6) Make up for the wages deducted for one month; (7) Allow the organization of a labor union; (8) Wages for substandard raw materials should be paid according to the daily wage; (9) Dismiss the stooge Chen Xiuzhen.

Attendees: The attendees yesterday included Xu Zhi from the Social Affairs Bureau, Wang or Xian, representing the Public Security Bureau, Wang Zhixin, as the recorder, Tang Jinying, Gu Jinmei, Zhu Ying, and Wang Maozhen representing the labor side, and Amano, a Japanese national, Ya Shishuo, Inoue Shinpei, and Chen Renlin, a Chinese translator, representing management.

Mediation Process: Yesterday's mediation used a separate consultation method. Representatives from the two municipal bureaus repeatedly enlightened the management, and the management agreed to increase the original wage reduction of 40% by one-third. However, they firmly refused other items such as paying wages during the strike and stated that if the labor side insisted on an increase, they would rather close the factory.

Labor's Concessions: The two representatives of the government informed the labor side of the management's attitude. The labor side insisted on the previous demands but expressed a willingness to compromise on the wage reduction, but insisted that it must still be at least 30 cents per piece. Otherwise, they would insist to the end and would never be subdued by the management.

Meeting Results: Since the attitudes of both parties were so irreconcilable, the two representatives of the government solemnly declared that since the two parties were so irreconcilable, the matter would have to be submitted to the municipal government for arbitration. Upon hearing this, the Japanese national stated that he was willing to reconsider. In the end, the Japanese national volunteered to convene labor representatives for direct discussion and then report to the Social Affairs Bureau. He also inquired with the Social Affairs Bureau representatives about the procedures for closing the factory. Mr. Xu informed him that if he wanted to close the factory, he would have to follow the labor union law and pay severance pay to the workers based on their years of service, one month's salary for each year of service, and half a month's salary for each year of service for those with more than ten years of service. If the factory is temporarily closed, it should not exceed two months at most and should pay each worker one-third of their wages. As for the direct negotiations between the factory and the labor force, the labor representative must have more than seventy people to be legal. Finally, the management agreed to reply on Monday before dispersing.

Explanation of Interest on Shareholders' Dividends

No Interest Paid if Not Claimed After Notification

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Hatters Association yesterday, stating in response to the previous letter inquiring whether interest should be paid on dividends due to shareholders of commercial firms if they are not claimed in a timely manner. After a detailed investigation by designated personnel, it has been found that it is customary in this city that shareholders of commercial firms are entitled to receive dividends as soon as they receive the dividend statement or notification slip. If they delay claiming the dividends, it means that they have voluntarily given up their rights, and there is no possibility of paying interest. Moreover, after the commercial firm has allocated dividends, the funds are stored in cash to await payment and cannot be used for other purposes, nor can there be any possibility of doing business. A corresponding letter is hereby issued in reply, for your reference.

Case of American Soldier Pushing a Chinese Worker to Death

Seamen's Union Submits Case for Negotiation

A U.S. Navy sailor on the (GnAm) gunboat in Hankou recklessly pushed Huang Xianbiao, a lighterman, into the river, causing him to drown. The Hankou branch of the Seamen's Union previously requested the Hankou Municipal Party Department to instruct the government to order the Public Security Bureau to investigate and reply, which was confirmed. Recently, the branch submitted the reply from the Party Department and a copy of the original report from the bureau to the China Seamen's Union for forwarding to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, urgently requesting the ministry to send a special commissioner to inspect Xiang, E, Chuan, Wan, and Gan and the Hankou Municipal Government to seriously negotiate with the American consul in Hankou in accordance with the post-settlement methods of abolishing the negotiation bureau, in order to obtain punishment for the murderer and compensation for the deceased. The report from the Hankou branch of our union stated that the case of U.S. Navy sailor (GnAm) throwing Huang Xianbiao, a lighterman, into the river, causing him to drown, was previously submitted to your union and the Hankou municipal party and government authorities for review and handling. Now, Order No. 1986 from the Hankou Municipal Party Department Rectification Committee states that the report from the union regarding the case of a U.S. Navy sailor on the (GnAm) gunboat throwing Huang Xianbiao, a lighterman, into the river, causing him to drown, requesting negotiation, was previously forwarded to the Municipal Government and instructed to be recorded. Now, Public Letter No. 504 from the Hankou Municipal Government states that the report from the China Seamen's Union Hankou Branch regarding the death of Huang Xianbiao, a lighterman, who was pushed into the river by a drunken U.S. Navy sailor on the (GnAm) gunboat, requesting serious negotiation with the American consul, has been forwarded to the Bureau for investigation. The Bureau has been instructed to forward it to the American consul for investigation, reply, and handle. The case was previously reported by the Public Security Bureau and the Hankou Seamen's Branch, and the circumstances were roughly consistent. The case involves the drowning of a Chinese national by a foreign sailor and cannot be ignored. The original report from the Seamen's Branch was copied and sent to the Public Security Bureau, ordering them to quickly send personnel to investigate the truth of the incident and provide a detailed reply, with instructions to notify them. Subsequently, the Public Security Bureau reported on the investigation of the case and requested a review. The circumstances were generally consistent with the report from the Seamen's Branch. The case has been referred to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review and notification to the Commissioner for Inspection of Xiang, E, Chuan, Wan, and Gan and a letter has been sent to the American consul in Hankou requesting investigation and reply. The aforementioned letter should be copied and sent to the Public Security Bureau for information. The above should be approved, and the Bureau should copy the original reports and order them to be informed. The two original reports from the Public Security Bureau were attached. It is appropriate to prepare a document along with the two original reports from the Public Security Bureau for your union's review and approval. It is hereby notified that the investigation of the case described in the two original reports from the bureau has been witnessed by the boatman Lao Huang Yuting, the watchman Luo Jinheng, and the owner of the World Shipping Company, Baiman, and they can prove that the matter is real. There is no doubt about it. The foregoing is hereby prepared and the original reports from the bureau are copied and forwarded to your ministry, urgently requesting the telegram to the Hankou Municipal Government to seriously negotiate with the American consul in Hankou in accordance with the post-settlement methods of abolishing the negotiation bureau and the Commissioner for Inspection of Xiang, E, Chuan, Wan, and Gan, to punish the murderer and compensate the deceased to comfort the souls of the wronged and maintain national dignity. Please advise.

"Antarctic Exploration" Premieres at the Grand Theater

Invaluable in Modern Historical Materials

The Grand Theater at No. 21 Museum Road premiered the rare film "Antarctic Exploration" yesterday. It is a photo of the voyage to the Antarctic by the world-famous explorer, U.S. Navy Rear Admiral Richard Byrd. The Paramount Company, known worldwide, sent two photographers with courage and insight to work with the team. They went through terrifying waves, icebergs, and snow, disregarding their own safety to achieve their goal. They shot more than 20,000 feet of film, of which only 8,000 feet were the best. It is an extremely grand spectacle. All of the icebergs of the Southern Ocean, the towering trees, the whales and seals living on the ice, the unseen Antarctic precious birds "Skua" flying in the Antarctic, and the hardships of the team members' exploration from beginning to end, as well as the loyal dogs who swore to live and die together, are all captured as much as possible. Watching this film inspires ambition and patriotism. At the premiere the other day, when British and American audiences saw the national flag flying in the Antarctic, they applauded and cheered. In order to increase the knowledge of students, the theater will add a show at 10 AM today. Students and children wearing school badges will be charged only 60 cents, regardless of their age.

Chen was arrested, and the opium was confiscated and taken to the police station. Yesterday, they escorted him to the French Public Court to prosecute. Chen confessed to smuggling opium. Education News

Important News

Principals of Primary and Secondary Schools in Jiangsu Province

Petition for Collective Resignation

Regarding the Assistance of the Abduction of the Principal of Suqian Middle School

Ren Zhongmin, Xie Jizeng, and forty other principals of provincial middle and primary schools in Jiangsu Province, regarding the case of Xiao Mingqin, the principal of Suqian Middle School, being unreasonably beaten and robbed by the garrison troops, for more than a month, the military and political authorities have not yet taken any considerable measures of punishment. They feel that principals have no protection when performing their duties, and everyone is in danger. Therefore, a few days ago, all the principals held a meeting in Zhenjiang and decided to resign collectively to express their support and to urge the military and political authorities to severely punish the officers and soldiers who committed the crime as soon as possible to uphold justice. Yesterday, the letter of resignation was sent to the Department of Education after being signed and sealed by all forty principals. The original letter is recorded as follows:

The petition is regarding the arbitrary looting of public funds and property by garrison troops, and the harming of public officials. Afterwards, there is no progress in punishment, and instead, there is retaliation. With power prevailing and justice not upheld, people feel endangered and education has no protection. We cannot maintain our positions and respectfully request approval to resign and the appointment of capable individuals. According to the case investigation, on August 19th, Xiao Mingqin, the principal of Suqian Middle School, was returning to school from the provincial capital on official business and was intercepted in Qingjiangpu by troops under Huang Meixing, the head of the 266th Regiment of the 133rd Brigade of the garrison. He was falsely accused of being a bandit, severely beaten, and paraded through the streets, losing the school seal and more than a thousand yuan of school funds. A petition had already been submitted to your department for forwarding to the provincial government and a detailed report to the military authorities, requesting a thorough investigation, severe punishment of the perpetrators, and compensation, as well as strict orders to all troops in the province to provide real protection for public officials in order to respect education and uphold the law. Afterwards, Principal Xiao repeatedly received instructions from your department and resolutions from the provincial government to order the brigade to punish the perpetrators and provide compensation separately. However, Liu Hanzhen, the brigade commander, according to the report of Huang Meixing, the regimental commander, completely denied the past facts of the case, falsely accusing Principal Xiao of beating soldiers and embezzling public funds, fabricating facts and defaming his reputation. The regimental commander even disregarded the law, giving the chairman of the provincial government one week to summon the parties for confrontation, or else he would take appropriate measures. The brigade commander also immediately forwarded the document and stated, "Confirmation by telegram is accurate," without any hesitation. The provincial government, regarding the reports from both sides, issued instructions to your department for a thorough investigation, but did not order the responsible military authorities to take responsibility. It is heard that your department has ordered the magistrate of Huaiyin County to investigate, but the county magistrate is facing many obstacles under the coercion of the regiment. How can he conduct a thorough investigation? At the same time, it is also heard that the regimental commander in Huaiyin has already intimidated all those who rescued Principal Xiao on that day and those who were identified as witnesses in Principal Xiao's submission, forcing them to testify against Principal Xiao and falsely claim that the entire incident was fabricated. If all these rumors are true, it is unknown what kind of effective measures the provincial government and your department will take regarding this case. It has been more than a month since the incident occurred. Principal Xiao has been recuperating from his injuries in the province and is gradually recovering, but the brain injury is too severe and it is uncertain whether he will fully recover. Because Suqian is close to the bandit suppression area of the regiment, and the regiment is unpredictable and tyrannical, there is no protection for personal safety once one enters the area. Therefore, while being concerned about the school, with the start of the school year and numerous affairs awaiting management, it is impossible to return to the school to perform duties. Even Huaiyin Middle School, Agricultural School, and other schools in Jiangbei, within or near the sphere of influence of the brigade and regiment, are constantly wary of this ferocious force and feel personally endangered, unable to serve with peace of mind. The fact that public officials are traveling on official business within the province, carrying public funds and property, is a common occurrence in all schools. Since the brigade and regiment belong to the National Revolutionary Army, where is the Heavenly duty to the people? How should their behavior and actions be different from bandits? After the incident, in terms of solving people's difficulties and upholding the law, what should be the difference between the situation in the revolutionary era and the situation in the warlord era? Considering the current situation, it is difficult to achieve any results in this case. The lives of public officials in the education sector of the entire province have no protection. We cannot maintain our positions and respectfully request approval to resign and the appointment of capable individuals. Respectfully presented to Chen, the Director of the Department of Education.

Explanation by the Ministry of Education on the Differences in Registration of Universities, Middle Schools, and Elementary Schools

The Ministry of Education, according to a report from the Guangdong Provincial Department of Education, stated that the Ministry had issued an order stating that school operators in various regions were neglecting regulations, resulting in many errors. Therefore, the key points of various regulations were selected and announced to the public for compliance to avoid errors. The announcement was issued to the Department for compliance and to inform the relevant departments for compliance and reporting for inspection. Upon investigation, the first section of the announcement, the procedure for reporting schools at all levels, item three, stated that after the board of directors has been approved for registration, it should immediately refer to the regulations, specifically Articles 20 and 24, and according to the level of the school established, follow the procedures listed in the regulations to submit an application for the establishment of the school, an application for the opening of the school, and an application for the registration of the school three years after the opening. However, the procedures stipulated in Article 20 of the Regulations for Private Schools are limited to private universities, independent colleges, and specialized schools. The procedures stipulated in Article 24 are limited to private secondary schools and higher schools. The statement in item three of the first section of the announcement, "Apply for school registration three years after opening," seems to encompass both Article 20 and Article 24 of the regulations, but it does not clearly distinguish between the three-year registration period for private universities, etc., and the one-year registration period for higher schools. As a result, many private middle and primary schools in various regions mistakenly believe that middle and primary schools must also wait for three years after opening before applying for registration. How should this be clearly explained or modified to avoid misguidance in handling? A document has been prepared to submit to your department for review and instructions for compliance. The Ministry of Education instructed the department, stating that the six characters "three years after opening" in item three of the first section of Announcement No. 3 of the Ministry refer specifically to private universities, independent colleges, and specialized schools. Because the original text regarding the registration period for private middle and primary schools was not explained and was easily confusing, the six characters "three years after opening" in this announcement were deleted in the compilation of the "Current Important Educational Laws and Regulations" published by the Ministry, page 160 of the General Rules. The registration period for private schools of all types should be handled in accordance with Articles 20 and 24 of the Regulations for Private Schools. You are hereby informed and instructed to inform all subordinates accordingly.

Since the National Government decided that one could not hold dual positions, important figures such as Jiang Menglin, Cai Yuanpei, and Dai Chuanxian have successively resigned from their concurrent positions as university presidents. Preparations for the Annual Meeting of the China Cooperative Society

The second annual meeting of the China Cooperative Society, which will be held in Hangzhou, is less than ten days away. The Preparatory Committee has largely completed the various preparatory matters. The latest news from the Society is excerpted below:

Proposals: The Society has received many proposals from members in recent days. The main points are recorded below: (1) Unify the names of various cooperative societies; (2) Centralize cooperative talents nationwide to study cooperative academics and promote cooperative undertakings (proposed by Yan Hengjing); (3) Request the National Government to promptly revise the Cooperative Society Law and promulgate it (proposed by Tong Yumin); (4) Establish an international cooperative marketing agency; (5) Request the government to order schools and mass education institutions to add cooperative courses and libraries to increase the purchase of cooperative books and newspapers; (6) Establish an advanced cooperative correspondence school affiliated with the Society (proposed by Ding Pengzhu); (7) How to promote rural consumer cooperation; (8) How to gradually make rural credit cooperatives independent; (9) Request the government to clearly define cooperative laws and regulations for compliance (proposed by Zhou Qihang); (10) The Society should expand its publishing department, organize a Chinese cooperative bookstore, and implement production to facilitate progress; (11) The Society should implement cooperative education to train cadres; (12) The Society should collect as many writings of members as possible to infuse the spirit of the Society and its members and promote cooperative operations; (13) The Society should use a second language to compile and send cooperative newsletters for international promotion (proposed by Wu Yuzhang).

Essays: Essays include Wu Juenong's "The Nature of Zhejiang Agriculture and the Cooperative Movement," Tong Yumin's "Rural Cooperativization," Zhang Tinghao's "The Protection and Future of Chinese Workers," and Hou Houpei's "Developing China's Foreign Trade through Cooperative Methods." Other essays, such as those by Wang Shiying, Wang Zhixin, Wu Yuzhang, Tang Qiyu, and Hou Zheyi, have been compiled and submitted to Shou Miancheng, the director of the essay department.

Circulars: The Preparatory Committee issued the third circular yesterday, stating: "Regarding the announcement of the reduced fare instruction for members' trips. All members who have returned reply slips have already received them when the second circular was sent out. Sports Promotion Association Should Apply for Registration with the Municipal Education Bureau

According to a report from the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, the Ministry of Education instructed the bureau, stating that the submission and attachments had been reviewed. Article 1 of the Measures for the Education Administrative Organs to Manage Academic Groups stipulates that "an academic group shall, in addition to complying with the provisions of the General Principles of the Civil Law and other laws and regulations, handle matters in accordance with these measures." Furthermore, the supplementary item of Article 7 of Section 3 of the Revised Scheme for the Organization of People's Groups stipulates that "Social groups shall comply with the provisions of special laws and regulations if there are special laws and regulations." Since the China National Sports Promotion Association is an academic group in nature, it should apply for registration with the bureau in accordance with the Measures for the Education Administrative Organs to Manage Academic Groups, in addition to fulfilling other required procedures. The request to forward the inquiry to the Ministry of Interior Affairs should not be discussed.

Chinese Win Two Championships at the Grass Court Tennis Tournament

Lin Qiu win Men's Doubles | Li Xinghua wins Women's Singles |

(1) Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai Win Doubles Championship

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai defeated Smith and Buddy yesterday at the French Club. The final result of the Shanghai Open Grass Court Doubles Tennis Championship was 7-5, 6-1, 6-3. Lin and Qiu won the championship. The umpire was Mr. White.

| Match Details |

The Shanghai Grass Court Doubles Championship began in 1911 and has been held for twenty years. In recent years, Chinese players have participated, but have failed to win the championship. This year, with the addition of Lin and Qiu, they have been invincible from the beginning and won the championship, bringing glory to the Chinese tennis world. Yesterday's final victory was quite easy.

The first set of the match was originally scheduled to begin at 2:30 PM, but because Lin Baohua arrived late, the match began at 3:00 PM. Lin arrived in a hurry and was unable to warm up comfortably, resulting in a significant reduction in his performance. Qiu Feihai was also affected by this and lost three consecutive games, causing dissatisfaction among the audience. Fortunately, from then on, their spirits were slightly revived, and they worked together wholeheartedly, leveling the score in an instant. After that, both sides competed tensely. The American team took the lead, and the Chinese team followed closely, keeping pace and refusing to give in. After 5-5, Lin's net play was ingenious and varied, and Qiu responded by consolidating the rear defense, making it impossible for the opponent to find any flaws. As a result, Lin and Qiu won 7-5.

In the second set, Lin and Qiu regained their original form, and all kinds of hitting techniques were skillful. In contrast, the opponents were flustered and frequently lost points. In an instant, they won four consecutive games. Smith and Buddy tried hard to counterattack and won back one game. Lin and Qiu continued to win two more games, and as a result, they won again 6-1.

In the third set, Lin and Qiu won the first game, and then Smith and Buddy took a 2-1 lead. Lin and Qiu added two games to take a 3-2 lead. Smith then struggled to catch up, only to tie the score. As a result, Lin and Qiu won 6-3. The final result was 3-0, and Lin and Qiu won the championship. Afterwards, Howard, the president of the Grass Court Tennis Club, presented two large silver trophies to Lin and Qiu, which they will keep for one year. The names of the two people are engraved on it as a historical commemoration.

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai, winners of the Grass Court Tennis Doubles Championship

(Photo by this newspaper)

(2) Li Xinghua Wins Women's Singles Championship

Unprecedented in the Shanghai Chinese Women's Tennis World

Defeated Feisi yesterday with a score of 6-4, 4-6, 7-5

In the final of the Shanghai Grass Court Tennis Club's Women's Open Singles Championship, our country's Li Xinghua played against Feisi at the French Club yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. As a result, Xinghua defeated Fei with a score of 6-4, 4-6, 7-5, winning the Grass Court Tennis Club's Women's Singles Championship.

Li Xinghua (left), winner of the Grass Court Tennis Women's Singles Championship, and Ms. Feisi (right), runner-up

(Photo by this newspaper)

Siezed the Championship, creating a new era in the Shanghai Chinese women's tennis world, and also a new record in the Grass Court Women's Singles Championship in eighteen years.

| Li and Fei's Skills |

Looking at the two players' skills, there is really no great difference. Xinghua is known for her agility and calmness, while Feisi wins with strength, and can use various hitting methods. Xinghua's backhand stroke is slightly weak, but her forehand stroke and chop shot are quite confident. The two fought fiercely. Xinghua was repeatedly in danger, but it was not easy to calmly and painstakingly turn the situation around. The more than three hundred spectators present were initially terrified for Ms. Li in the midst of the storm, but were finally able to celebrate her victory, which was even more gratifying and commendable. The umpire was Lin Baohua.

In the first set, Li Xinghua served first. The two returned the ball from the baseline, cautiously and without letting go. Xinghua took the lead, being agile and extraordinary, winning three consecutive games and creating an excellent opportunity. Feisi was unwilling to be outdone and quickly caught up. Xinghua also kept pace. The two had their own achievements, comparing from 3-0 to 5-3 and then to 5-4. Xinghua always had the upper hand, but Feisi's counter-attack was also very strong. The result of this set was Xinghua winning 6-4.

In the second set, Xinghua served and still won the first game. Feisi also added one game. In the third game, the two volleyed at the net, fighting bravely. After 2-2, Feisi's momentum suddenly increased, with her strokes to the left and right being very effective, causing Xinghua to run around and create a return with Feisi in the lead. Xinghua carefully fought back, like a piece of beef jerky. Feisi could not stand the battle and repeatedly extinguished her own power with improper force. Xinghua then caught up with two games, making it four each. At that time, Xinghua's ball momentum was very good, with a feeling of accomplishing everything in one breath. Unexpectedly, she lost the next game due to carelessness, resulting in a loss of 4-5. At this important juncture, Xinghua was extremely persistent and determined to retaliate. In the tenth game, Xinghua repeatedly faced dangerous situations, but was finally able to maintain a balanced situation. This game was fought for a total of 26 points before the victory was decided, with a score of 14-12 going to Feisi. As a result, the victory of this set also went to Feisi with a score of 6-4.

With the sets tied, the third set became a life-and-death decisive battle. The competition was fierce and the situation was tense. Xinghua still served first and won the first game. Feisi won two consecutive games to take a 2-1 lead. Xinghua also added two games. Feisi won again, becoming 4-3, and then 4-4. Xinghua followed closely behind. Suddenly, Feisi was about to win again with 5-4. In the next game, Xinghua was at a disadvantage with a score of 1-3. With only one point left, she was about to lose the whole game. At this critical moment, Xinghua suffered and persevered, escaping death and making it 5-5. The audience held their breath and broke out in a sweat. Afterwards, Xinghua seemed to see the sun after a rainstorm and her spirits were greatly boosted. On the contrary, Feisi seemed to be something in a bag that was taken away by others, feeling extremely frustrated. Xinghua took this opportunity to win two consecutive games and win the final victory with 7-5. After the match, the trophies were still presented by Howard, who said that Ms. Li's victory in this championship was truly a new era for Chinese women's tennis and was very commendable. Then, the silver cup was presented to Xinghua, and there was thunderous applause for a while. Xinghua shook hands with Lin Baohua, Qiu Feihai, and the Westerner Mr. White, and they all congratulated her.

Free Talk

A Word of Insight

— Zheng Yimei

The sun shines on the earth, and all things move, naturally arousing thoughts of fame and profit. The cool moon flows through the sky, without a speck of dust, naturally inspiring thoughts of transcending the world.

If there is Chang'e on the moon, then future Earth-Moon travel will stir up countless waves of love and romance.

It is the same autumn season, yet one may listen to it, or chant about it, or grieve over it, or be startled by it, depending on one's state of mind.

Those who are ashamed of wearing coarse cloth and sackcloth do not know those who eat sweet grains and meat are bitter about beans and water.

After a long period of cold and freezing, there must be warmth and harmony. Those who are in adversity should think like this.

To be truly rich is to be indifferent and without desire.

Those who speak well do not fall into clichés, and those who do things well leave no trace.

Quietness can be constant, and coldness can last for a long time. Movement and heat make it temporary.

Hold the rudder steady to prevent capsizing, and hold the heart steady to prevent damage to virtue.

Mountains and forests are enough to shelter my body, and books are enough to entrust my aspirations.

Writing is for the benefit of the world, not to flatter it. To flatter the world is worse than pleasing oneself.

In dealing with the world, one should leave room for maneuver; in eating and drinking, one should leave a lingering taste; in writing, one should leave a lingering meaning; in making music, one should leave a lingering sound.

Independence in the vastness has its own economy, and its own learning.

I have two pairs of tears: one to weep for the ancients when reading books, and one to weep for the people of today when reading newspapers.

In dealing with the world, one should leave room for maneuver; in eating and drinking, one should leave a lingering taste; in writing, one should leave a lingering meaning; in making music, one should leave a lingering sound.

Kang Youwei's Discussion on Foot Binding

— Cheng Zhizheng

Mr. Kang Youwei of Nanhai was outstanding in his articles, economic insight, and knowledge. He died in frustration because his reform failed. Occasionally reading his disciples' collected drafts of the 1898 reform, although only a dozen articles were collected, the novelty of his thoughts and the fluency of his arguments were enough to shock the ignorant. I once saw his memorial requesting the prohibition of women's foot binding, in which he described the suffering of women's foot binding in great detail. It said, "As soon as they are weaned and their hair has not dried, their muscles have not grown, and their bones have not hardened, their weak feet are bound horizontally with three feet of cloth and seven feet of ribbon. They bend their fingers to make them walk, break their bones to make them bend, and walk timidly and crouchingly on the ground. The young girls suffer and cry day and night, and some add medicine water to fumigate them day and night with narrow socks and small shoes that cannot be taken off at night, so as to make them bend without stretching and slender without strengthening. They get up by leaning on the bed and walk by leaning against the wall. The rich suffer from it, and the poor suffer even more. They personally operate the well and hold the mortar, take care of the weak children, and serve the sick mother-in-law. They come and go to report and run without stopping. When they go to deep places and climb high places, they sigh and sigh with sorrow and cover their faces with tears. Some fall to their deaths because of climbing ladders, and some are injured because of illness. As for water and fire, when there is chaos and they have to flee for their lives, carrying their husbands, holding their children, and carrying things and clothes, it is impossible to cross the streams and difficult to climb the high peaks. The roads are blocked by chaotic rocks and the clothes are hooked by thorns. Many hang themselves from trees and abandon their lives or fall from buildings and die." The description is so detailed and meticulous, truly the work of a genius.

Random Jottings from the Xuyuan Garden

— Tianxu Wosheng

Last Sunday, Little Butterfly was not back from Hangzhou, so I attended the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Factory on her behalf and had some thoughts. I will try to describe them below. Since the import of foreign goods, our country's native cloth has been overshadowed and has no place to stand. Many people have lost their jobs, which has had a regrettable impact on society. Now, if people in various villages and counties raise three to five thousand taels of silver to specialize in buying native cloth and transport it to Shanghai for artistic printing and dyeing, then its sales and uses will certainly not be inferior to Russian chintz. Although the texture is extremely rough, once it is printed and dyed, it can be transformed from ugliness to beauty, and it is durable. The cost of printing and dyeing each foot is only about one cent, which can be said to be extremely cheap. However, in terms of printing and dyeing, the machines run very fast, and they can print and dye about 300,000 feet per day. However, it takes a lot of time to change a printing plate, so it is most cost-effective to print 3,000 bolts of ten feet each. Otherwise, at least 600 bolts must be printed at a time. However, if it is distributed by counties, it can be matched evenly. For example, if sixty counties buy native cloth and specialize in this printed fabric business, they can gather in one factory for printing and dyeing, and the factory can be asked to match the colors. If each county has 600 bolts, the total number of sixty counties is 36,000 bolts, which can be printed and dyed in just half a month. The average distribution of each color means that each county can get 60 kinds of colors, with only ten bolts of each kind, to supply half a month of sales. The daily sales volume is only 40 bolts, which is about 4,000 feet in terms of feet. If the amount needed per person is ten feet, it can only supply the needs of 400 people. Assuming a year of durability, the county's population of 140,000 to 150,000 is enough to meet the demand, without having to seek external supply. The amount of native cloth sold and used in the local area each year can reach about 14,000 to 15,000 bolts. If we assume that each foot earns a profit of five li, then each bolt can earn a profit of five jiao, and the annual surplus profit can be more than 7,000 yuan. With a capital of three to five thousand yuan, such a surplus profit can be obtained. Even if money is borrowed for business, the monthly interest on 5,000 yuan is only 600 yuan. The remaining profit is still 6,000 yuan, which can be paid off in one year, which is quite easy. It would be even more appropriate to prepare new-style wooden machines and distribute them to weaving households to obtain uniform products. As for the bleaching and refining project, the printing and dyeing factory is responsible for its associated responsibility, so there is no need to seek self-reliance. In the past, when I tried to run the Butterfly Clothing Printed Silk Factory on a small scale, many counties sent letters asking to print native cloth, but the printing costs were not cost-effective, so I could not fulfill their wishes. Thinking about it now, the above plan can become a reality. There is no shortage of people in various counties who care about industry and are anxious to take action for the livelihood of women in their hometowns. Moreover, the printed colors can be guaranteed not to fade, and simple dyeing or bleaching or extracting white flowers from the entire surface is even simpler. It is best to print native cloth as willow crepe or wool-like, slightly like the newly released Freedom Cloth from the Sanyou Society, so that all the blemishes are covered by the colors, and it is suitable for both Chinese and Western clothing. Alternatively, it can be printed as the flower chintz style used on furniture and woodenware, taking its durability and beauty to replace coarse twill cloth, so that its sales will also be wide and will surely be welcomed by society. The factory is currently printing and dyeing machine-woven products and has not yet touched native cloth. I have this feeling, but I am afraid that there will be many people who are eager for quick success and few who sympathize.

Minor Recipes

— Yang Yixiao

Grape Balls: Take fresh grapes, remove the pits, dry them in the sun, mix them with flour, and fry them in oil until golden brown on both sides. They are sweet and sour and delicious.

Pomegranate Zongzi: Open the pomegranate, remove the skin, take the seeds, wrap them with glutinous rice in reed leaves. Pomegranates are a symbol of having many children. Wrapping this zongzi is most suitable for sending to the wedding of a Qian family.

Lily Crisps: Put lilies in a pottery pot, stew them on a charcoal stove until they are well cooked, then stir-fry them with dry flour and lard, mix them well, add a little white sugar and dried fruit, and knead them into crisps. They are exceptionally soft and loose.

Banana Rice: Peel the bananas, put them in a stone mortar, and mash them with a pestle. Take glutinous rice and lard, put them in a large bowl, steam them until cooked, and then add longan meat and other ingredients on the outside. The flavor is quite beautiful.

A Record of Visiting Chen's Farming and Reading Garden

— Li Shi

I have heard the name of Chen's Farming and Reading Garden for a long time and have wanted to visit it, but I have not been able to find a companion. On the seventh day of this month, I was invited by Mr. Chen Cuiheng and Mr. Xu Juying, so I went with Mr. Chen Junjie, Zhifen, and more than 20 members of the Youth Federation.

The garden is located in Jiangwan, thirty miles north of Shanghai, far from the city and isolated from the noise. The gate faces a small stream, the water of which is clear and can reflect objects. The garden has many mountains, and the mountains have many trees of different kinds. The garden has many ponds, and the ponds are full of blooming water chestnuts and lotus, which are splendid and dazzling. When the breeze comes, the flowers and leaves sway, and the ripples ripple. One can relax and enjoy oneself while traveling in it. Mr. Chen farms and reads here and has found his place. Then, after going around the garden, we rested under a pavilion. There were many stones around the pavilion, and the stones were stacked to form a mountain, which was towering and high. Some of my companions sat on the top of the mountain, some lay under the pavilion, some got up and ran races, and some leaned and sang songs. The forms were different, and the attitudes were different. Later, Mr. Chen Hongguang initiated a game of placing forty kinds of miscellaneous objects on the table, each person was limited to observing them for two minutes, and after reading, they wrote down what they had read one by one, limited to fifteen minutes to turn in the papers. The one who remembered the most kinds without errors would get an apple and a pear. In the end, Mr. Chen Gunian won the prize with 30 kinds. Immediately, laughter and applause rose one after another. It was noon, so we took out the fruits we had brought and shared them together. After eating, we strolled on the lawn, which was as green as a carpet. Occasionally, we heard the melodious music and the mournful sound of insects, which had a special meaning. Suddenly, the sound of the bugle was made in succession, so we went back to our seats together. Mr. Chen Suikang suggested making a humorous question and answer. If the answer matched the answer in the question, a banana would be awarded. The fun was unconstrained, and the imagination was wonderful. After that, he initiated a competition to take notes from each other. For example, four people, A, B, C, and D, stood at a distance of about two zhang (approximately 20 ft) from each other. An impartial person took a section of an article and read it aloud twice. A heard it and told it to B, B told it to C, C told it to D, and D recorded it one by one and handed it over to the impartial person. The winner was determined by the speed of the time and the number of typos. This kind of mutual transmission of notes can be said to be a wonderful way to pass the time. Then, the sun set in the west, and our pleasure came to an end, so we returned. After returning, my heart lingered, as if I was still attached to the beauty of the mountains, rivers, forests, and valleys, and I could not let go for several days, so I wrote this down with a pen.

Brief News: The famous actor Cheng Yanqiu has already landed at the Huangpu Pier on the 26th on the Tianjin Maru and is staying at the Fanwang Palace. It is scheduled to visit the gentry and business circles on the 27th and to meet with ticket sellers. He will perform on stage at the Rongji Grand Theater on October 3rd. The first day is "Yu Tang Chun", the second day is "Bi Yu Zan", and the third day is "Si Lang Tan Mu" (Songxue).

Acknowledgement and Introduction: Mr. Zheng Gengyun of Zheng Jingshantang Pharmacy on Sanma Road, Yunnan Road, has inherited a good ancestral prescription and produces five major holy medicines: Wanying Huaizhong Bao, Shenxiao Zhitong Bing, Women's Health Tablets, Shaqi Emergency Relief Powder, and Bodhi Oil. They have long been popular in Guangdong and Guangxi and in various ports in Nanyang and are famous everywhere. Yesterday, I was given a copy of each as a gift, so I hereby express my thanks and introduce them.

Miscellaneous Notes on the Great Catastrophe in Changsha (Part 2)

— Litian

I remember that there was a candy shop run by a father and son in a street in Caichao Gate. They had been in business for many years, but someone reported that they were very wealthy. The Red Army Division and Department sent people to arrest the father and extort 12,000 yuan. The son was so anxious that he could not think of any way. He calculated that if he could sell all the shops and land, he could only get more than 4,000 yuan, and who would want to buy these real properties at that time? So, crying, he ran to the Red Army Headquarters to explain that he was willing to hand over all his property and ask to release his father. The Red Army refused. He even volunteered to redeem his father with his own body, but the Red Army still refused. Two days later, they killed the old man in his sixties.

The spear squad was even more ferocious in killing people because they did not kill people quickly and happily in one fell swoop, but stabbed a few spears casually. There were also several different shapes of spears, and the most deadly was the spear with a hook. When this kind of spear was stabbed into the chest and abdomen, the heart, liver, and internal organs would be torn out. It was pitiful that the head was on the neck and could not be out of breath for a while. Those who were killed with spears had to be delayed for at least several hours or even more than ten hours before they died. On Zhongshan Road, a middle-aged woman holding a child was killed in this way. The child was snatched away by the spear squad, and the woman screamed in pain on the road for half a day before she died.

All retired civil and military officials and people with some property were among those who were searched and killed. These searches and killings, except for some very famous ones, relied on the denunciation of local thugs. Among them, there were indeed many who sought revenge, but even more innocent people had their entire families searched and killed. The most incomprehensible thing was probably the mansion of a certain public figure who was very famous in Hunan. His house was very large and known to everyone, but this time the communists not only did not burn or loot this only large mansion, but also posted a notice on the door: "Anyone who burns or robs this house will be executed by the Third Army of the Red Army."

Commander-in-chief Peng Dehuai" It is said that this notice was very responsible, and indeed the mansion of a certain public figure stood alone.

Brief Biographies of Overseas Chinese in San Francisco (Part 1)

— Kang Kang

Within ten steps, there must be fragrant grass; in a village of ten households, there must be loyal and trustworthy people. Moreover, there are more than 20,000 overseas Chinese in San Francisco, who have multiplied and thrived for three or four generations, and talented people emerge in large numbers, making it difficult to count them all. However, most of them return to their motherland or are distributed to various countries. Here, I will only briefly mention a few people who live in the overseas Chinese area for a long time and are quite prestigious, just to give a glimpse of an example.

Tang Bang: Those who travel in the overseas Chinese area of San Francisco cannot but take Shenfa Company as the center of their destination. Shenfa is the earliest and largest bone and Su department store here. Its architecture slightly imitates the Chinese style and has the beauty of tall pavilions and flying eaves. The owner is Tang Bang from Taishan County. He is over seventy years old, obese and hunched over. His crown and shoes are simple and plain. Those who see him do not know that he is a millionaire. The store sells Chinese goods of all sizes, but in recent years, it has also mixed in Japanese goods. There are dozens of young girls as receptionists, wearing gorgeous Chinese costumes that illuminate the wayfarers. His daughters and granddaughters, more than a dozen of them, are all stunning beauties. Last year, due to international love issues, the newspapers advertised and the court litigated, and it is still unresolved. It is said that Mr. Tang, although he is extremely frugal in his own lifestyle, has many internal pets, and there are many illegitimate children who are raised and nourished, filling the family. The property disputes in the future should be even more intense.

Zhou Song: Among the new generation of capitalists in the overseas Chinese community, Zhou Song from Xiangshan should be regarded as the best. Fifteen years ago, he was still an employee in a clothing store. He established a Yiyuan Company, specializing in selling men's and women's clothing and supplies, with a value of no more than one yuan. He started his business with this and became rich. Now he has established more than a hundred branches in California, and there are agents, brokers, factories, and stores in various western provinces. A total of 7,000 Chinese men and women are employed, all of whom are from Xiangshan. Westerners also call him Zhou. He is only in his forties, generous, and likes to give alms. He is generous in donating to public welfare and private friendships. Those who know him and those who do not know him praise him a lot.

Cotton Market Shows Promising Signs in the Afternoon

The cotton market was flat in the morning but firm in the afternoon. However, the American cotton market is showing a clear downward trend. Yet, the local cotton situation is still firm because the farmers in various regions are unwilling to release their cotton. A large number of domestic merchants are buying up cotton, believing that the local harvest will be poor. The amount of cotton being taken in remains consistently high, hence the tight market. However, due to political unrest in India, yarn factories have stopped work, causing a surplus of raw materials, which are being aggressively sold abroad at reduced prices. As a result, various factories are buying large amounts of Indian cotton, completely encroaching on the position of Chinese cotton.

The closing price was as high as 2 yuan, 4 jiao, 7 fen, and 2.5 li, which is significantly higher by 1 fen and 2.5 li compared to the previous day's closing price. The price of October also rose by 5 li. The price of the forward date was also initially good, then returned to its decline as the factory sold the short, and the final price of November, Positive November, and February was the same as the closing price the previous day, and that of December was down by 2.5 li.

Wheat Futures Continue to Fall by Two Fen

This Month's Deliveries Were Clear, With Only Huafeng Taking in Four Cars

After the opening of the wheat market yesterday, it continued the weakening trend of the previous day, and prices for all months fell by 3.4 fen. Then, because the flour market reported a rise, sentiment turned positive, and prices for all months rose by 2.3 fen. However, the actual sales of spot wheat were still very sluggish, and there were large shipments of foreign wheat, and there was no real sales activity of flour and wheat, so it was difficult for the market price to stand. As a result, the prices of October fell by 2 fen, those of November by 2 fen, those of December by 1 fen, that of January was unchanged, and that of February fell by 1 fen. The current month's deliveries have been completely delivered, and there are many reports of verification and release of goods. Due to the lack of receiving households, only Huafeng Factory took in four cars, and the rest were settled at a price to offset the price. The spot wheat market is still sluggish. Yesterday, the transaction price for a car of high-grade wheat was 4 yuan and 7 jiao, and the price for 2,000 bags of Shashi wheat was 4 yuan, 1 jiao, 4 fen, and 5 li, and the price of Shashi wheat was slightly higher by 1 qian, 3 fen, and 4 li compared to the previous opening price.

Foreign Wheat Fell by Two or Three Jiao According to Yesterday's Telegram

Yesterday, the Tongxun Agency's 8:45 telegram reported that Chicago's September wheat futures were 7 yuan, 6 jiao, and 6.25 fen, the same as the previous day; the December contract was 8 yuan and 3.75 fen, down 2 jiao and 6.25 fen from the previous day; the March contract was 8 yuan, 6 jiao, and 7.5 fen, down 3 jiao and 5 li. Also, Canadian wheat futures for September were 7 yuan, 2 jiao, and 1.25 fen, also down 2 jiao and 3.75 li from the previous day; December was 7 yuan, 4 jiao, and 6.25 fen, down 2 jiao and 6.25 fen; and March was 8 yuan, 1 jiao, and 2.5 fen, down 2 jiao and a half.

Yellow Beans Fell, Sesame Seeds Remained Weak

After the price of yesterday's standard Liaodou (soybeans from Liaoning) dropped sharply by 1 qian from the previous day, customer appetites became slightly active. In the afternoon, after receiving a telegram from the Lian Electric Company reporting flatness, the situation became more stable. Therefore, the December contract still opened at 4 yuan, 9 qian, and 3 fen, and the January contract at 4 yuan and 9 qian. The market has a sign of a short-term recovery. The source of spot beans from the Yangtze River has gradually arrived from various locations. Initially, due to the standard being extremely small, people were watching. Then, due to the sale by cargo customers, the market became stable. As a result, there was not much rise or fall in the market price from the previous day. It is estimated that 1,200 bags of Tianjin Jinyuan, 200 bags of Jiujiang Chidou (late beans), 150 bags of Jiang Qiaozi, and 350 bags of Hankou Zaohuang (early yellow beans) were sold.

The sesame seed market has remained flat in recent days. Because the harvest in the inland has been abundant, shipments to Shanghai have been very frequent, and the accumulation in the city has gradually increased. Foreign firms have little business, except for slight movement in Europe and the United States, and Japan is even wanting to reduce sales, leading to few transactions. Prices have remained relatively stable. Shashi, Hankou, and other white sesame seeds are still around 8 yuan and 3 jiao and a half. Jiujiang milk sesame, Yuan sesame, and Xue sesame are only between 7 yuan and 7 jiao and 7 yuan and 4 jiao. A total of 950 bags were sold for the day.

Reduced Arrivals of Customer Xian Rice, Temporarily Stable

Yesterday, the arrival of customer Xian rice was scarce. The appetite of both local and country merchants has been good, and the market has been temporarily stable. However, the number of Du rice entering the market is increasing, and Xian rice from all locations has been launched onto the market. Xian rice from various ports above Nanjing is waiting to be loaded down south, and the harvest in Jiangxi, Anhui, and Hunan provinces has been good. Although it has not seen very robust arrivals now, arrivals from Shen (Shanghai) are eventually expected in the future. Furthermore, there are also confirmed orders for foreign rice arriving in port, and people are still bearish as a result. Although the arrival of customer Xian rice was scarce and sales were active yesterday, the market price remained stable, but there is still no good outlook for the future market. 1,000 bags of Jiangxi machine early (rice) were sold, priced at 11 yuan, 2 jiao, and 4 fen to 10 yuan and 6 jiao, 100 bags of early brown rice were priced at 8 yuan per jiao, and 300 bags of Wuhu machine rice were priced at 10 yuan, 6 jiao, and a half to 10 yuan and 1 jiao.

Sugar Market: Cotton Lake Red Sugar Still Thinly Inventoried, Market Still Attractive

Price Setting and Transactions Quiet, Market Weak

Yesterday, the sugar market's place of origin (Cuba) telegraphed that the current price of Cuban sugar was 1.09375, which had fallen 3125. The price of New York's December sugar futures was 1.06, down 5 points; the price of next year's March sugar futures was 1.16, and the price of May's was 1.23, each also down 6 points. The Association's market had a setting price on Dutch sugar #24 coarse granulated white, but purchasing interest was still scarce, and transactions were even quieter because it was Saturday. New cargo was transacted slightly at 8 yuan and 5 fen. Chen cargo (old cargo) was rare at 7 yuan and 7 qian, and the demand for Shouzhong (hand selected) granulated white was also quiet at 7 yuan and 9 qian. Nissho N mark was 8 yuan and 1 qian, J mark was 8 yuan, 2 qian, and 2.5 fen, Minghua YT mark was 7 yuan and 9 qian, YRO mark was 7 yuan, 8 qian, and 2.5 fen, and TM mark was 7 yuan, 7 qian, and 2.5 fen. Imports and exports were also sparse, and the market shape still felt weak. Haopan (listing of sellers) had domestic unified hand rock sugar listed for dozens of boxes, priced at 1 yuan and 6 liang, and the market saw flatness and weakness. Cotton Lake red sugar continued to be listed for 40 bags, priced at 1 yuan and 8 liang and 5 qian. Because the market inventory was particularly thin, the market was still attractive.

North and South Goods Hainan Dried Longan (Guiyuanrou) Haopan (Listing of Sellers) Fell Again

Since the new Guiyuanrou product came out this year, the price has frequently declined because the go-around market has been flat. Hainan Yuanrou has been the most numerous for cargo out, so the price fall has also been the greatest. The previous listing was as low as 26 liang, then it rose to 27.8 liang. Because the arriving source was prosperous again, this unusual trend was rekindled. It was previously heard that 400+ pieces were listed, with higher-grade goods priced at 26 liang and 2 qian, and ordinary goods priced at 25 liang and 7 qian, all of which require losses to costs. Shengshai (sun-dried) Yuanrou also fell one or two liang up and down, but Shijie (stone boundary) Shengshai Yuanrou has a small number of arrivals, so the price is still stable.

Silk and Tea Factory Silk European Sales are Unmoving

Shanghai Foreign Firm's Silk Sales Still Have No Life. Inspecting European and American Silk Weaving Factories, to Reduce Expenses For Raw Materials, Outside Of Artifical Silk and Low-Priced Japanese Silk, Italian Silk and Two Countries Silk were deemed too expensive, with no purchasing power. European Sales of Silk Factory is Completely Stopped. Yesterday, Boxingsheng entered Hehua brand top #28-30 sliver head, Pot Wash Yellow Silk Reeling with 8 packages priced at 651 liang, and Gaobei entered Earth Brand Top #2 Washing with polluted yellow coarse silk with 10 packages priced at 285 liang.

Artificial Silk Future Rises, Current is Flat

Artificial silk sales have been booming recently. Many domestic manufacturers need large number of artificial silk. Transactions are very frequent. 150 count goods from Germany, France, Italy are sold specially well. According to information from foreign bank, artificial silk company fixed price are hard, and stock price has been reduced more than 20% compared to last month. Based on current prices, the cost of artificial fiber is much more expensive than the last month. However, the artificial silk sales is must be booked early to prepare for silk spinning early next spring, but vendors insist on delivery in future, but will accommodate prices for spot goods. This has caused the market to rise. Prices for each hundred pound has risen between two liang to five/six liang. Manufacturers only trade in Futures, because Autumn silk already spun, artificial silk will not be mixed for winter goods production. Spot trades are slow, and Futures trades are active, and Futures trades are popular, with the largest amount traded around December to prepare silk cloth for weaving of silk "hua si ge", crepe, zhongshan crepe and early spring silk cloths.

Lakes and Rivers Region Autumn Cocoon, 3000 packages, Transported to Shanghai via waterway

The lakes region, Wu Xing, Changxing, Deqing and other counties have kept their Autumn Silkworm capacity, however there was damage due to the weather being unfavorable. Production is expected to be only 30-40%. Silk merchant shops that are open are only 40%. Not enough production for the Shanghai factories, so factories are now requesting waterways and small boats. Estimated amount 3000 packages or so to be transported to Shanghai.

China Tea Russian Sales Will Be Revived

Notice of starting a Tea program next week

Since Russian stores and Association have stopped business, Shanghai Tea market has been desolate. From reliable source, Russian traders who had been working in Hankou are now free to the Shanghai bank Association for Gongxi Green tea and Ningzhou Red Tea. It's been decided to start business next week, with plans announced for Zhenmei Green Tea and Morocco sales still sluggish. Market is still not doing well.
