Shanghai Market

Business News

Yongshengchang Cigarette Shop, located at the entrance of Pintang Lane on Nanjing Road, proclaims that the shop has been established for many years. Due to the renovation of the building, it has moved to the central part of Pintang Lane and reopened for business on the 24th of this month. It continues to operate as usual, and the prices of various cigarettes and cigars are especially low. In recent days, there has been a huge influx of customers. The various brands of Pisi (a type of cigarette) sold are selected by the shop owner himself from Yongding, Fujian, so the taste of the tobacco is palatable and has long been praised by smokers. Recently, they have further improved and refined the production, and the products are even better than before.

Zhong Qihua Company on Nanjing Road proclaims that the company's piece goods department and shoe department have new, fashionable autumn and winter goods arriving in abundance. As the weather is gradually getting colder, the company is holding a special sale on these two departments. The fashionable velvet-like fabrics, flower-patterned broadcloth, Western-style velvet, men's and women's woolen fabrics, and other items in the piece goods department are particularly outstanding. Furthermore, there is a clothing material discount department with cheongsam materials priced from 80 cents to one yuan or one yuan and fifty cents. Flower-patterned fabrics are priced at one yuan for four to six yards. In the shoe department, the black leather men's shoes are the cheapest at five yuan and fifty cents per pair. The yellow leather-trimmed children's shoes are one yuan and eighty cents per pair. Black

Page 28

Leather-topped rubber-soled children's shoes are one yuan and eighty cents per pair. Men's and women's tennis shoes are 25% off, American Michelin tennis shoes are 20% off, and foreign men's and women's leather shoes are 15% off. All kinds of boots, shoes, and equipment are cheap, and the quality is excellent. It is no exaggeration to say that valued customers are welcome.

Xiyuan Hengyong Silk and Satin Store in Huajin Lane, Second Ma Road, proclaims that the store's major business focuses on patterned and plain ceremonial banners. Since the beginning of business this spring, the store has been known for its exquisite products, prompt service, and low prices, and has been praised by customers. As a result, business is booming, and the store has become a leader in the industry. Recently, following commercial custom, the store officially opened on the 22nd of this month and held a sale. To commemorate the occasion, the store invented a new type of silk ceremonial banner called "Economic Banner," which is sold at nine jiao per banner to thank customers. In recent days, the sales volume of this type of banner has been very large.

Huilo Company, located at the corner of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road, proclaims that although the company has recently renovated its facade, all departments are still operating as usual. Yesterday, the men's Western clothing department received a large shipment of autumn supplies. Various fashionable and high-quality woolen hats, woolen socks, colorful woolen artistic scarves, cashmere gloves, Western and Chinese-style raincoats, woolen sweaters, and various high-quality sports shirts, fashionable sweaters, neckties, stiff collars, and soft collars are all exquisite and lovely, and the prices are lower than those sold in the market. There are also leather-faced Western-style overcoats with fine workmanship and durable materials. The academic and military communities, as well as senior military officers, have purchased them and consider them to be the best leather-faced overcoats.

Lehua, Chunqiu, Wenyi, Guangming, Mingyue, and other bookstores in this port proclaim that in order to spread culture and promote business, they have rented a building next to the Zhonghua Book Company on Fourth Ma Road to establish a joint sales department. The decoration has now been completed and is scheduled to open today (the 28th). There will be a grand sale for three weeks and many gifts to commemorate the occasion. A grand event is expected at that time.

Page 29

The Stationery Department of Wing On Company proclaims that the stationery department's business is extremely developed, which is rare. The department has always adhered to the principle of small profits, so customers from far and near flock to it. Recently, a large batch of display and decoration supplies has been shipped from abroad, which are extremely complete and most suitable for celebrating the Double Tenth National Day. There are dozens of kinds of beautiful paper lanterns, each priced from half a jiao to one yuan and a half. Flower garlands are priced from one jiao to one yuan and two and a half jiao per bundle. Other items such as paper strips, paper flower edges, printed crepe paper, beautiful paper lampshades, imitation paper flowers, flower baskets, five-color crepe paper, national flags, party flags, and world flags are extremely complete and the prices are very reasonable.

Qiwen Silk Weaving Factory proclaims that the factory has been established for five years and specializes in selling silk woven landscapes, portraits, calligraphy, colorful flowers, and business cards that are lifelike, elegant, and exquisite. The factory has won awards in various competitions and is sold both domestically and abroad. Purchasers have praised the factory around the world. Now, on the occasion of the fifth anniversary and the opening of a branch in Hongkou, a grand sale will be held for one month. Whether it is woven pieces or picture frames, a discount will be offered. Large orders will receive even more preferential treatment. Detailed catalogs can be requested by mail or obtained in person. The addresses are Nanjing Road, east of Hongmiao, and south of Peng Road on North Sichuan Road.

Theater News

The Great World proclaims that Japanese national Sato Tomiharu is able to eat poisonous snakes, centipedes, spiders, rats, dogs, and all kinds of poisonous raw plants without harming his life, attracting the attention of society and providing a valuable reference for the physiological community. The Great World has invited him to perform, and the audience is extremely crowded every day. The people of Shanghai are curious and want to see what is going on. Sato chooses the most poisonous snake, crushes its head with his teeth, and swallows it. The viewers are all amazed and exclaim. There are not many days left for the performance, and he will be leaving Shanghai soon.

Sanxing Stage proclaims that Mr. Zhou Bingchen, the manager of the stage, has observed the psychology of the people of Shanghai and, together with Mr. Zhao Ruquan, the backstage manager, has repeatedly planned and reorganized the stage. It reopened on the 20th and has re-equipped the interior with scenery and painting. In addition, it has been changed to a mixed performance by men and women, so the stage's entrance has been extremely crowded recently, and it has been sold out before the opening.

Medical News

Zhengfeng Medical Lodge, located on the west end of Simalu, opposite the Shanghai Stage, proclaims that Liu Hanqin, a Confucian scholar from a family lineage in Taixing, is a famous person. He possesses extremely profound knowledge of both Chinese and Western learning. His family learning is deep-rooted, and he has studied medical principles for ten years and practiced medicine clinically for ten years. Although he has served as the chairman of the county education association and the speaker of the county assembly, he must still spare some time after official duties to fulfill his obligations and provide consultations. All cases that other doctors find hopeless, such as wind-heat, damp-heat, cholera, malaria, and dysentery, as well as male, female, and pediatric ailments, and all external and internal injuries, and difficult miscellaneous diseases, will be cured upon diagnosis and treatment. Currently, due to many affairs in his hometown, he has yielded to the request of friends and accompanied Ma Bingqian, a specialist in Jinzhen Ophthalmology, to Shanghai to practice medicine at this medical lodge. Mr. Ma is a disciple of the late famous Taizhou doctor Mai Runzhi, inheriting all his secrets. All external and internal eye obstructions, lymphatic toxicity attacking upwards, infantile malnutrition, eye injuries, cloudy eyes, inverted eyelashes, pterygium, and other severe conditions that other doctors cannot cure can be effectively treated by Mr. Ma using acupuncture, grinding, cutting, and topical application. Furthermore, Liu and Ma are particularly skilled in treating consumptive diseases, asthma, and coughs, providing immediate relief from eye pain.

Shen Bao Pictorial Weekly

(1) Dr. Wu Chaoshu, the chief Chinese representative to the 11th League of Nations Assembly and Minister to the United States, is pictured with his wife in a car en route from the United States to Europe.

(2) The PEN International Annual Congress was held in Warsaw in late June. The person with the creative hairstyle in the picture is the reporter and Chinese representative, Mr. Guo Zixiong.

(3) The German Institute of the University of Berlin hosted diplomatic and foreign circles. Mr. Jiang Zuobin, the Chinese Minister to Germany, is on the right in the middle. Mr. Luther, the former German Interior Minister, is in the center.

(4) Mr. Ong Chgo.hu, a native of Huilai, Guangdong, graduated from the Japanese military academy last year and went to France to study aerial combat tactics. He was elected chairman of the Chinese-French Aviation Research Association. On July 24th, when ascending to 500 meters, the propeller was damaged, and the aircraft crashed, breaking three high-voltage power lines. The entire plane was shattered, but he only suffered minor injuries and did not die, demonstrating his superb skills. Therefore, the French newspapers competed to report him as a "brave Chinese man." — (Xiao An)

(5) Dr. Xie Shou Kang, the Chinese Chargé d'affaires to Belgium, paid tribute and laid flowers at the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier in Belgium on August 11th. The Belgian government specially dispatched Lieutenant General Bandu to greet him. The person in military uniform saluting is in the picture.

(6) The Tenth International Penal Conference was held in Prague on August 25th. This is a group photo of representatives from various countries in front of the conference hall. The person in the center (X) is the chairman, the Czech Minister of Justice Mr. S. The three people at the top in the middle are the Chinese representatives, from right to left: Mr. Ke, the government representative; Mr. Xie Weiqin of the embassy; and Mr. Jing, the representative from the Central Research Institute.

(1) The Northeast Military Academy held its graduation ceremony on September 9th. Sitting in the center is Zhang Xueliang. To his right is Mr. Tang Shikui, the chairman of Liaoning Province. Mr. Zhou Lian, the dean of the academy, is to his left, and Mr. Yuan Jinkai is to his left.

(2) The west gate of Taian was blown up with explosives. The debris is now being cleared to restore traffic. — (Guo Hanping)

(3) An express train on the South Manchuria Railway from Changchun to Dalian derailed at the Ma Po River station on September 3rd. The chief of works died, and a driver was injured. Passengers were quite alarmed. — (Northeast News Agency)

(4) Tan Yankai, the acting chairman of the National Government and Premier of the Executive Yuan, passed away suddenly from a stroke on the morning of September 22nd. The government ordered the national flag to be flown at half-mast and suspended entertainment for three days to mourn his death and will hold a state funeral. The image above is the bronze statue of Mr. Tan, sculpted by Jiang Xiaolan during his lifetime.

(5) Regarding the signing of the London Naval Treaty, the Japanese government is dissatisfied with the Cabinet's arbitrary actions and is holding a thorough investigation meeting. However, due to the lack of support from the elder statesmen, it was passed on September 17th. Therefore, the current cabinet has overcome a difficult situation and does not need to resign. This is the situation of the cabinet discussing measures to deal with the government. The person wearing Western clothes is Prime Minister Hamaguchi Osachi.

(6) In the French Concession of Hankou, two gun emplacements have been built near the front and rear of the police station, each about five feet high and capable of holding four machine guns. Those walking in the area are wary. — (Chen Daqing)

(7) This year marks the 25th anniversary of the Russo-Japanese War. Japan's victory over Russia elevated it to one of the five great powers. A grand commemorative event was held in Tokyo. This is a picture of warships parading through the city.

(8) Ms. Meade, a reporter for the New York Tribune, came to Guangzhou to promote the International New Religion (Baha'i Movement) and gave a speech. This is a photo taken when she was accompanied by Mr. Forrest, the director of the Guangzhou Municipal Forestry Bureau, to visit the Municipal Library. — (Zhao Bangfu)

(9) The National Private Electrical Association recently held a conference in Nanjing. This picture shows the luncheon at the Central Hotel on September 5th. Sitting at the left and right ends facing outwards are Mr. Shen Sifang and Mr. Li Yanshi, who recently returned from the World Power Conference. — (L)

(10) Due to overproduction in the United States, the number of unemployed people is increasing daily. Recently, the New York City government specially established a free employment agency run by experts. On the first day, fifteen hundred men and women went to register.

(1) This is a scenic view of the New Territories of Hong Kong. The sails and the shimmering water are so beautiful! The British government occupied Kowloon and then expanded to Baoan County. The foothills of the Shenzhen railway station have been demarcated as the New Territories. It is about ten miles from Kowloon to the New Territories. The mountains are steep and deep into the interior. A ring road and a coastal pier have now been built, and a medical clinic has been established. Looking at the dozens of villages in the boundary, one cannot help but sigh at the beautiful rivers and mountains. — (Tang Shixian)

(2) Swimmers at the Lai Chi Kok swimming pool in Kowloon. This is one aspect of the life of local women. — (Guo Xichou)

(3) The Biwu pool in Moganshan has clear water. Swimming there is especially wonderful. — (Zhu Xinye)

(4) The Qiantang Tidal Bore is one of the famous scenic spots in Zhejiang Province. The time for viewing the tidal bore this year is approaching, and it is expected to be larger than in previous years. Therefore, the Water Conservancy Bureau has designated several areas along the seawall in Haining as viewing spots for the tidal bore. — (Zhou Yushan)

(5) Boating on the lake at the Rio Rita Villa in western Shanghai. The people in the picture are photographer Ms. Ouyang Huifang and her friends.

(6) The first swimming competition of the Inter-College Swimming Association of Jiangnan University was held at the new swimming pool of Jiaotong University on September 21st and 22nd. As a result, Jiangnan University had the best overall results, followed by Great China University, and then Guanghua University. — (Yu Kai)

(7) The beauty of the Rio Rita Villa in Shanghai lies in the water, which can be used for swimming and boating. The person standing at the pier is Ms. Wang Jihui. — (W)

(8) Sun Island in the heart of the Songhua River in Harbin is a popular summer resort. Every holiday, tourists flock there to enjoy boating and swimming. — (Wang Yanshi)

(9) A watercolor painting by Mr. Pan Entong, a member of the Baie Painting Society in Bupu.
